About Attock Campus
COMSATS University Islamabad (former COMSATS Institute of Information Technology) started its Attock Campus in 2004 and since then it has been offering undergraduate and graduate programs in Computer Sciences, Management Science, Electrical Engineering and Mathematics. CUI Attock is becoming the regional center of excellence in providing education in sciences and business administration and the graduates of CUI Attock are currently serving in various organizations, both in private and public sector

Scholarships And Financial Aid
The
Students Financial Aid Office (SFAO)
at COMSATS University Islamabad (CUI), Attock Campus, is dedicated to ensuring that financial constraints do not hinder talented students from achieving their academic goals. We manage a diverse range of internal and external funding opportunities. All of these scholarship available subject to the announcement of the concerned department / agency.

You’ll find something to spark your curiosity and enhance your journey as a COMSATS University Attock alumnus in Pakistan
As a prominent graduate of COMSATS ATTOCK, I have earned recognition in domain of Sales Management, presently working with NESTLE as Regional Sales Manager. My academic journey at CUI Attock shaped the skills that defined my professional growth.
Muhammad Ali Malik
Regional Sales Manager, NESTLE
As a distinguished alumni of COMSATS ATTOCK, I have build a reputation in field of Administration, currently serving Pakistan Aeronautical Complex as Deputy Director HRM. My BBA Honrs from CUI Attock laid the foundation for my success story.
Fahmida Kanwal
Deputy Director HRM PAC Kamra
As a renowned alumnus of COMSATS ATTOCK, I have built expertise in Technical Consulting, currently serving ITS Australia as Lead Technical Consultant. My academic experience at CUI Attock shaped the skills guiding my professional growth.
Sharjeel Sana
Lead Technical Consultant, ITS. Australia

Examinations Office
Examinations Office
Office of Deputy Controller of Examinations is headed by Mr. Mehr Yahya Durrani Deputy Controller of Examinations CUI Attock and is fully responsible for smooth conduct of examination related activities. Main functions Office of Deputy Controller of Examinations are as under:
To enhance the efficiency of Examination Department under the supervision of worthy Director and Controller of Examinations.
Provide guidance to all the stakeholders regarding examination rules and regulations.
Conduction and supervison of the sessionals and Terminal Examination.
Notifying the Date sheet.
Declaration and Notification of Semester Results.
Issuance of progresive results card to the students.
Verfication of Transcripts and Degrees.
Issuance Circulars and Notices regarding various examination activities.
Counsel students / parents about improvement of grades.
Controlling of Unfair Means.
Conduction of Convocations of graduates.
Horizontal and Vertical communication.
Team
Mehr Yahya Durrani

Introduction

Introduction
About University
COMSATS University Islamabad (former COMSATS Institute of Information Technology) started its Attock Campus in 2004 and since then it has been offering undergraduate and graduate programs in Computer Sciences, Management Science, Electrical Engineering and Mathematics. CUI Attock is becoming the regional center of excellence in providing education in sciences and business administration and the graduates of CUI Attock are currently serving in various organizations, both in private and public sector, in small and large scale organizations. The graduates of CUI are the real ambassadors and evidence of the quality of education, we provide.
There are approximately 2650 students enrolled in and more than 60% of the students are studying under various scholarships schemes from provincial and the national governments and foreign donor agencies.
# 664 Ranking 2026
Quacquarelli Symonds (QS)

University Mission Statement
The COMSATS University Islamabad envisions assuming a truly national character for itself in the years to come. It envisions having presence in all provinces of the country. It sees for itself a position among the top five (5) universities in the country; among top 100 universities in the developing countries and top 500 universities in the world respectively in the 5, 10 and 15 years time horizon. Focus in the period 2005-10 has been on science led engineering; in the period 2010-15 on initiating social sciences programs and in the period 2015-20 will on establishing programs in medical and agricultural sciences.
University Vision Achievement
The COMSATS University Islamabad founded in the belief that understanding enriches all people, is dedicated to the search for truth through advancement of learning and extending the frontiers of knowledge; to the sharing of this knowledge through education in an academically diverse range of disciplines and subjects; and to the application of this knowledge to benefit the people of Pakistan in particular, and the Muslim Ummah, and the world, at large.
We are passionate about education and dedicated to providing high-quality resources for learners from all backgrounds in Pakistan

Facts and Figures
Established in 2004
Departments 05
11,600 Library Books
Current Student's Enrollment 1956
10 Undergraduate 6 Graduate and Doctoral 5 Programs
So far, over 1,800 Research Papers have been Published in HEC Recognized  Journals.
A total of 21 fully Equipped Laboratories Support Computer Science, Electrical & Computer Engineering, and Management Sciences Programs.
The Campus Operates 8 Buses Covering Key Routes Including Rawalpindi/Islamabad, Wah/Taxila, Hazro, Nowshera, Fateh Jang, and POF/Sanjwal
Hostel Accommodation Available For 100 Male & Female Students
The Campus Offers a Basketball Court, Cricket Ground, Football Ground, Hockey Ground, & a Fully Equipped Gym Plus Table Tennis Facilities
The Campus Mosque Accommodates Over 300 People For Friday and Eid Prayers, With a Separate Prayer Gallery For Female Students
The Campus has 3 Parking Areas 1 for Students & 2 For Faculty & Staff Accommodating Up To 100 Cars & Bikes
With a Strong & Growing Network of 6,250 Alumni, Over 3,311 Graduates are Proudly Registered With Our Community. Among them, 1,744 are Successfully Employed in Diverse Fields, Including 32 Who are Building Careers Abroad
The Campus Features CCTV Surveillance, Dual WAN ISPs With 24/7 340 Mbps Internet, & a Fiber Optic LAN Connecting Buildings at Up to 10 Gbps With Server Rooms

CUI Leadership

CUI Leadership
CUI Leadership
COMSATS University Islamabad (CUI) started its journey in 1998, and established its first campus at Islamabad in April 1998. In August 2000, in recognition of CUI´s achievements, the Federal Government granted it the status of a Degree Awarding Institute (DAI) through promulgation of its charter. The CUI is now slated for upgradation as a university by the name of ‘COMSATS University’ through an Act of the Parliament.
Vision
COMSATS Islamabad Campus adheres to the philosophy of getting the stamp of excellence in the field of Science and information technology and becoming self-sustaining state of the art academic and research institute and leading solution provider.
We aspire to produce unparalleled individuals who contribute to the world through their research and knowledge.
December 20, 2025
Message From The Rector
Dear Students, Faculty Members, and Visitors. It gives me great pleasure to welcome you to COMSATS University Islamabad (CUI), Attock Campus an integral part of a vibrant multi campus university...

Department of Computer Science
WELCOME TO
Department of Computer Science
About Us
The mission of the Computer Science Department at CUI Attock is to provide degree programs and courses to meet the full range of needs of the talented students in the area of Information Sciences and Technology. Departmental programs are based on a common core curriculum and rationally demanding courses designed by leading experts that supports the breadth of the discipline.
More Read
Our Leadership
Message from the Head of Department CS
It is a matter of pride and pleasure for me to introduce the Department of Computer Science, COMSATS University Islamabad, Attock campus. Sitting squarely in the Faculty of Information Science...

Department of Electrical Engineering
Home
Department of Electrical Engineering
WELCOME TO
Department of Electrical Engineering
About Us
The Department of Electrical Engineering (EE) in Attock campus was established in 2007. The EE department aims to achieve academic and research excellence in the subject area through its well-designed curriculum, strong focus on research and innovation, objective based learning and strong industrial liaison.
More Read
Our Leadership
Message from the Head of Department EE
Since inception, the department has been producing world class graduates and postgraduates. The state of the art infrastructure and lab facilities are established with grants from different agencies which ensure...

Department of Computer Engineering
WELCOME TO
Department of Computer Engineering
About Us
With a vision to produce professional engineering graduates, the Department of Electrical Engineering was established in 2007. The EE department aims to achieve the academic and research excellence in the subject area through its well-designed curriculum, strong focus on research and innovation, objective based learning and strong industrial liaison.

Department of Mathematics
WELCOME TO
Department of Mathematics
About Us
The Department of Mathematics, COMSATS University Islamabad, Attock Campus, established in 2011, is a dynamic centre for mathematical studies at undergraduate and graduate level. Initially the Department started a 2 years MSc Mathematics program in Fall 2011 and later on MS Mathematics program was inaugurated in Fall 2012.

Bachelor of Science in Computer Science
Home
Undergraduate
Bachelor of Science in Computer Science
Bachelor of Science in Computer Science BS(CS)
Mission Statement
The mission of the CS program is to provide high quality education in computer science that prepares students for professional careers and lifelong learning in developing / managing computational processes and systems, with emphasis on systems automation, information management, management of IT infrastructure and Intelligent Systems.
Program Educational Objectives
To meet the needs of our constituents, our Program Education Objectives state that within a few years of graduation our graduates will have:
Demonstrate a sound understanding of the main areas of the body of knowledge and the theories of computer science, with an ability to exercise critical judgment across a range of related issues.
Critically analyze and apply a range of concepts, principles, and practices in net-centric computing, information management, management of IT infrastructure and intelligent systems; showing a range of problem solving skills and effective judgment in the selection and use of corresponding tools and techniques.
Demonstrate the ability to work as an individual with minimum guidance and as a leader/member of a team.
Follow appropriate practices within a professional, legal, and ethical framework.
Identify mechanisms for continuing professional development and life-long learning.
Career Outcomes
Computer science is primarily concerned with information processes, the structure and procedures to represent them, and the systems for their implementation. Advancements in technology mean there is no shortage of need for computer scientists in today’s world. Training in computing and software development can take you to technical positions or open the door to many other careers, too. The following list provides some examples of positions a computer scientist might hold: Computer Programmer, Computer Engineer, Hardware Engineer, Information Systems Analyst, Software Engineer, Systems Analyst, Data Communications Analyst, Programmer-Analyst, Telecommunications Specialist, Computer Security Specialist, Computer Support Specialist and Teacher. Graduate student critical thinking, analysis, research, and creative problem-solving skills are highly valued in a variety of fields.
Eligibility
Students are eligible for admission if they have Intermediate or equivalent
(‘A’ Level)
with minimum 50% marks from accredited institution and
*NTS-NAT
test score with minimum 50% marks.
* Detailed information can be obtained from
http://www.nts.org.pk

Bachelor of Science in Electrical Engineering
Home
Undergraduate
Bachelor of Science in Electrical Engineering
Bachelor of Science (BS) in Electrical Engineering
Program Overview
The Bachelor of Science in Electrical Engineering (BSEE) program started in Fall 2007. The Electrical Engineering program at COMSATS University is designed to provide students with core knowledge and skills in Electrical Engineering with specialization in Power, Telecommunications, Electronics, Computer and Controls.
The Electrical Engineering program nurtures its graduates to be competent in professional practice and fulfill the technological needs of society in an ethical, moral, and socially responsible manner. Moreover, the students are trained to communicate effectively and show management and entrepreneurial potential. The students are engaged in life-long learning to continually enhance personal and professional capabilities.
The curriculum, labs, workshops, and industrial placements equip the students with the latest tools and techniques relevant to national and international industry. The Department of Electrical and Computer Engineering has an active industrial advisory board which continually provides feedback on our curriculum in relevance to the current industrial requirements.
Process for Admission and Admission Criteria
Progressive development up the ladder of knowledge in an engineering program hugely depends upon quality of students at induction stage. CUI not only ensures the minimum criterion laid down by PEC but also requires candidates to appear in competitive exams to ensure equality among country wide student base. National Testing Service (NTS) entry test is given due to weightage apart from past academic records while determining merit for admission in bachelor of science in electrical engineering. Admission to Bachelor of Science in electrical engineering is determined by admission office based on open merit.
Admission Criteria and Response
As per the PEC criteria it is mandatory that candidate must have 60% marks in F.Sc. (Pre- Engineering) / equivalent qualification and must qualify the entry test for admission in engineering programs. Details of admission criteria implemented in CUI under the guidelines of PEC are as under:
NTS Test 50%
HSSC/A Level / DAE (relevant field) 40%
Matriculation/O-Level 10%
Program Educational Objectives (PEOs)
PEO 1:
Demonstrate competence in the professional practice of Electrical engineering.
PEO 2:
Fulfill the technological needs of society in an ethical, moral, and socially responsible manner.
PEO 3:
Exhibit an ability to function and communicate effectively as an individual or team member and show management and entrepreneurial potential.
PEO 4:
Engage in life-long learning to continually enhance personal and professional capabilities.
Program Learning Outcomes (PLOs)
PLO 1:
Engineering Knowledge:
An ability to apply knowledge of mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and an engineering specialization to the solution of complex engineering problems.
PLO 2:
Problem Analysis:
An ability to identify, formulate, research literature, and analyze complex engineering problems reaching substantiated conclusions using first principles of mathematics, natural sciences and engineering sciences.
PLO 3:
Design/Development of Solutions:
An ability to design solutions for complex engineering problems and design systems, components or processes that meet specified needs with appropriate consideration for public health and safety, cultural, societal, and environmental considerations.
PLO 4:
Investigation:
An ability to investigate complex engineering problems in a methodical way including literature survey, design and conduct of experiments, analysis and interpretation of experimental data, and synthesis of information to derive valid conclusions.
PLO 5:
Modern Tool Usage:
An ability to create, select and apply appropriate techniques, resources, and modern engineering and IT tools, including prediction and modeling, to complex engineering activities, with an understanding of the limitations.
PLO 6:
The Engineer and Society:
An ability to apply reasoning informed by contextual knowledge to assess societal, health, safety, legal and cultural issues and the consequent responsibilities relevant to professional engineering practice and solution to complex engineering problems.
PLO 7:
Environment and Sustainability:
An ability to understand the impact of professional engineering solutions in societal and environmental contexts and demonstrate knowledge of and need for sustainable development.
PLO 8:
Ethics:
Apply ethical principles and commit to professional ethics and responsibilities and norms of engineering practice.
PLO 9:
Individual and Team Work:
An ability to work effectively, as an individual or in a team, on multifaceted and /or multidisciplinary settings.
PLO 10:
Communication:
An ability to communicate effectively, orally as well as in writing, on complex engineering activities with the engineering community and with society at large, such as being able to comprehend and write effective reports and design documentation, make effective presentations, and give and receive clear instructions.
PLO 11:
Project Management:
An ability to demonstrate management skills and apply engineering principles to one’s own work, as a member and/or leader in a team, to manage projects in a multidisciplinary environment.
PLO 12:
Lifelong Learning:
An ability to recognize the need for, and have the preparation and ability to engage in, independent and life-long learning in the broadest context of technological change.
Curriculum Overview
The core courses are designed to develop complex engineering problem solving skills of students in the areas of power, signal processing and communications, embedded systems, IoT, software programming, digital system design, control and automation, AI and machine learning.
The students also take courses in humanities, management and social sciences to enhance their soft skills. In the final year of studies, the students are required to complete a capstone project in which they demonstrate their knowledge and skills gained during the course the program. The students are cognizant of the UN SDGs and are required to target a set of SDGs in their final year project.

Career Prospects
Our graduates are in high demand in industries ranging from automation, power, defense, telecommunications, software and IT. The major advantage of the Electrical Engineering program is that our graduates have versatile skills in the national and international job market. Our alumni are employed in various national organizations including NTDC, Huawei, SkyElectric, Nayatel, PTCL, Telenor, Ufone, Mobilink, Wapda and renowned international organizations.

Bachelor of Science in Computer Engineering
Home
Undergraduate
Bachelor of Science in Computer Engineering
Bachelor of Science in Computer Engineering BS(CE)
Entry Requirements:
Intermediate or equivalent with Physics, Mathematics, and Chemistry having minimum of 60% marks or DAE in the same discipline of engineering with minimum of 60% marks from an accredited educational institution Valid NTS test score as per CUI policy.
Duration:
Minimum: 8 Semesters; 4 years Maximum: 12 Semesters; 6 years
Credit Hours Requirements:
Minimum 135 Cr. Hrs.
Offering Semester:
Fall (Attock)
Offering Campus:
Attock
Program Information:
In many countries, including the developed ones, the acute shortage of computer engineers is being felt and it is estimated that in next five to ten years the scarcity of computer engineers will reach a critical stage With this scenario in mind and the inevitable addition of more power generation units to be set up in Pakistan, CUI felt the need to offer Computer Engineering program of undergraduate level.

Bachelor of Science in Business Administration
Home
Undergraduate
Bachelor of Science in Business Administration
Bachelor of Science in Business Administration BS(BA)
Mission Statement
To inculcate the understanding of business fundamentals in the undergraduate level students that will facilitate them to capitalize and later specialize in growing areas of Business Administration.
Program Overview
Already enjoying a good reputation among employers, our BS(BA) or BBA program gives students a rigorous insight into business administration from both a holistic as well as methodological perspective. Emphasis is placed throughout the program on grooming the personality of our students and sharpening their communication skills. CUI expects that it’s students not only be thoroughly familiar with all essential and current business concepts and practices, but are also able to think analytically and innovatively and, above all, to judiciously apply their acquired knowledge in practical situations they may encounter in a professional context after their graduation.
Our BBA program spans 133 credit hours and includes course modules in all major business administration subject areas. In addition, CUI offers a large number of electives from which our students can freely choose. If you are looking for high quality business education at a very affordable price, then try CUI’s BBA program.
The minimum duration for completion of BBA Degree is eight semesters and a maximum of twelve semesters. It is awarded on completion of 133 Credits hours with a minimum CGPA of 2.0/4.0. Furthermore, the students also complete an internship of three credit hours.
The BBA Program is focused on four major areas of specializations;
Marketing
Finance
Human Resource Management
Information Technology Specialization
Special features and objectives
The objectives for this degree program are to:
Familiarize students with the fundamental bodies of theoretical and applied knowledge of business represented in the core courses
Provide students an opportunity to learn new tools and techniques in areas such as accounting, marketing, and management as represented in upper level courses
Enable students to integrate formal academic learning with their business related experiential learning
Encourage self-improvement and professional growth among students
Expose students to the global business environment.
This program prepares them to proceed onwards to a more targeted Master’s program in the fields of Business Administration, Public Administration, Economics, Project Management, Quality Management, Energy Management, Banking and Finance, Marketing, Human Resource and Social Sciences.
Admission and Eligibility
Session:
The programs are offered in Fall (September) and Spring (February) Session
Qualification:
Intermediate or equivalent (‘A’ Level) with minimum 50% marks from accredited institution is required.
Test and Score:
NTS-NAT test score with minimum 50% marks.
Duration & Semesters:
The minimum duration for the completion of the degree is eight semesters (04 Years) and a maximum of twelve semesters (06 Years).
Documents Required:
Following documents must be attached with the admission form:
Demand Draft in favor of CUI Islamabad Campus from any bank.
MATRIC / O-Level mark sheet certificate & Equivalence, (photocopy back to back).
FA/FSc / A-Level mark sheet, certificate & Equivalence (photocopy back to back).
BA/B.Sc/B.Com/BBA (2 years) mark sheet, certificate & Equivalence (photocopy back to back) for BBS applicants only.
Copy of NIC / B form.
Valid NTS Result (photocopy) [if test already given].
Paid original copy of NTS Challan Form, [if NTS test not given].
Hope Certificate/Affidavit (To be notarized on Rs. 20/- Stamp Paper) mandatory for result awaiting applicants only.
Undertaking (To be notarized on Rs. 20/- Stamp Paper) mandatory for all applicants.
Attendance
is a serious business and 80% attendance is mandatory to be eligible for examination.
The Students must be on the rolls of CUI and have registered for the course.
The student is now allowed to sit in the examination if he/she fails to reach within 30 minutes from start time of paper
Student
ID Card
and
Admit Card
is Mandatory in all examinations.
No Written Material, Scientific Calculators, Digital Diaries, Mobile Phones etc are allowed in Examination Hall.
If a student tries to use unfair practice the following penalties can be imposed to him/her.
Fine up to Rs.20,000/-
Cancellation of Entire Examination Result
Expulsion from The Institute
Rustication from The Institute
You Should Know
A
semester
means 15-18 weeks teaching, excluding examinations. There are two regular semesters per academic year at CUI.
One credit
hour means at least one hour teaching per week throughout the semester.
A full time student
means a student who has registered at least 12 credit courses in the semester.
Grade Point Average (GPA)
is the weighted average of the grades earned in the courses during a semester.
Cumulative Grade Point Average (CGPA)
is the weighted average of the grades earned in the courses during a program.
Discipline
in the campus has to be maintained. Any act of indiscipline is liable to punishment to the degree of severity of the act.
A student is placed on
PROBATION
if his/her CGPA is less than 2.0
If a student earns two consecutive probations, he/she
CEASES
to be a student of the institute.
A student can
DROP
(although not desirable) a registered course, within the specified time, but he/she will not have to pay its course fee when it is re-taken. The last date for drop of course is mentioned in the semester schedule.
A student can
WITHDRAW
a course before the second Sessional but will have to pay the fee when it is retaken. The last date for withdrawal of courses is also mentioned in the semester schedule.
We are serious about:
Punctuality and Timeliness
Focused Attention
Mobile phones must be switched off in class
No SMS messages written or received
No misbehavior will be tolerated in class!
CUI takes very serious note of any cases of cheating or use of “unethical means‟ during examinations.
Written project assignments submitted to the instructor may be subjected to a “plagiarism check‟ using anti-plagiarism software provided to CUI by the Higher Education Commission of Pakistan.
CUI is a
NO SMOKING
Campus

Bachelor of Science in Mathematicsathematics
Home
Undergraduate
Bachelor of Science in Mathematics
Bachelor of Science in Mathematics
Mission Statement
Bachelor of Science in Mathematics (BS in Mathematics) is offered by all the well-known public and private sector Universities of Pakistan. It is equivalent to Master in Mathematics (MSc) offered by our department. The objective of this program is to make all the students capable to conduct research or possess appropriate, cogent and tangible knowledge in Mathematics, to prepare graduates with enhanced skills, knowledge and attributes that will be needed for a successful career and professional accomplishments after graduation. This will able the graduate to use mathematical tools and language to understand the physical world around us. BS Mathematics is four years/8 semesters/133 credit hours degree. Students will be required to carry out course work comprising of subjects from mathematics, computer science, social sciences, humanities, environmental sciences, and physics.
Program Objectives
To understand and apply general and specific concepts and uses. So that they can demonstrate mastery of fundamental mathematical concepts that encompass calculus, statistics, algebra, and analysis etc.
Reason logically, think critically and connect mathematical ideas, in particular by being able to construct proofs and reason abstractly. So that they can read and write in the discipline and communicate mathematical ideas.
To produce professionals with strong mathematical back ground.
Prepare the graduate to use mathematical tools and language to understand the physical world around us
Expose students to the global Mathematical Research environment both in pure and applied Mathematics.

Master of Science in Computer Science
Home
Graduate
Master of Science in Computer Science
Master of Science in Computer Science MS(CS)
Mission Statement
To inculcate research culture in the students and cope with the growing trends of research in the field of computer science. This program will enable students to undertake research in by understanding the theoretical foundation of computer science coupled with knowledge of latest trends in this domain.
Program objective
Provide detail study about theoretical foundation of courses in computer science.
Enable student to undertake research in the field of computer science.
Understanding the latest trends in various sub domains of computer science such as
Computer Networks
Software Engineering
Databases
Distributed Computing
Machine Learning
Data Mining
In depth learning in one sub domain of computer science
Work effectively as team member for undertaking research in a specific cluster.

Master of Science in Electrical Engineering
Home
Graduate
Master of Science in Electrical Engineering
Master of Science in Electrical Engineering MS (EE)
Program Overview
The world is rapidly progressing, and technology has become an essential part of our lives. Electrical Engineering is a field that plays a crucial role in shaping the technology of today and tomorrow. With new innovations emerging every day, pursuing a Master of Science in Electrical Engineering can open doors to several opportunities in this exciting field. The MS Electrical Engineering of the EE Department offers a comprehensive and advanced program in Electrical Engineering. The Electrical Engineering program at EE Department offers students opportunities to work on cutting-edge research projects, gain experience of addressing the real-world problems in their research and develop a professional network at national as well as international level that prepares them for global careers. Graduates of this program are well-equipped to pursue a variety of career paths in related fields both in Pakistan and around the world.
The primary objective of our graduate programs is to impart education and training to a student in interest for pursuing graduate studies, to inculcate the spirit of learning in the student, and enhance his/her research orientation, critical thinking, research analysis capabilities, hypothesis testing and report writing skills. The following streams are offered in the program.
Research Opportunities
The Master of Science in Electrical Engineering has the following nine streams:
Computing and Electronics
Communications and Networks
Electric Power and Smart Grid Systems
Control and Automation
Machine Learning and Artificial Intelligence
Internet of Things
MS Program Structure
The scholar must complete a minimum of 30 credit hours for MS degree, out of which he/she has to undertake minimum 24 credit hours of course work and 06 credit hours of MS thesis/Research Project.
The scholar can register a minimum of 03 credit hours and maximum of 12 credit hours in a semester.
The scholar can register an alternate elective course from the approved list of elective courses of the program in case the failed elective course is not being offered by the respective department.
The scholar can register for research thesis after completion of 12 credit hours of course work, on the advice of the Supervisor/Supervisory Committee/Graduate Advisory Committee.
Admission Criteria
For MS
A 16 years degree in the relevant field from an accredited educational institution with First Division (annual system) or CGPA 2.5/4.0 (semester system).
No third division or D grade throughout the academic career.
GAT (General) with 50% marks.
Curriculum Overview

Master in Business Administration
Home
Graduate
Master in Business Administration
Master in Business Administration MBA
Program Overview
An MBA 1.5 years is a graduate level program provides an opportunity for business professionals having a four years bachelors degree in business related disciplines to obtain a Graduate Level degree i.e. Masters in Business Administration.
The one and a half years MBA program will meet the increasing demand for advanced business education which will not only combine text book learning with case study methodology but will expose students to an environment which will facilitate development of there conceptual skills as well as personal growth. This program is designed for those who want to have better career prospects after obtaining a graduate level professional degree (according to the HEC Roadmap for Business Education). The MBA program builds on the strengths of our experienced faculty who come from well-reputed International organizations/universities and offer rigorous studies.
Special Features and Objectives:
This MBA program will equip motivated and dedicated professionals who are ambitious to take up influential positions in the well reputed organizations with a blend of core knowledge of business and management principles obtained at a graduate level degree program.
It will help enhance business and management knowledge from the ground up via core courses that refresh student’s existing skills and understanding of key topics. This program covers extensiveness of knowledge across every discipline of business and management and would develop transferable skills. The MBA 1.5 years program offers much more than business fundamentals in a collaborative environment. The participants will learn new ways to think about the problems, and will gain the resources to help solve them.
The MBA 1.5 year’s program graduates will have gained the analytical skills, understanding, and the know-how to lead and to create and implement strategy at all levels in an organization. By the end of program, the students will feel comfortable taking up leadership and decision making roles to can work across disciplines and cultures to manage change, develop creative solutions to problems and improve performance and be innovative. The students take their learning back into the workplace – immediately and practically.
Program Content:
The MBA 1.5 years program will equip and develop strong management and interpersonal skills with the sound technical knowledge-base, required in today’s dynamic business environment. Courses in this MBA program are designed to introduce students to the various areas of business sand management. The program is designed to offer flexibility with choices of electives, concentrations and projects.
The MBA 1.5 years program consists of 36 credit hours taught during 3 semesters and includes seven compulsory course modules in all major business administration subject areas.
Issues in Accounting Practices
Applied Marketing Strategies
Managerial Economics
Quantitative Business Analysis
Financial Decision Making
Corporate Social Responsibility
Seminar in Public and Business Policies
In addition three elective courses are offered to choose from. The MBA Program is focused on major areas of specializations i.e. in the fields of Marketing, Finance, Human Resource Management, Logistics and Supply Chain Management. The students also must submit Graduate level project or thesis as part of degree completion requirements.
Eligibility:
A 16 years degree in the relevant field from an accredited educational institution, with minimum First division (annual system) or CGPA 2.5/4.0 (Semester System) and no third division (annual system) or D grade (Semester System) throughout the academic career. NTS GAT (General) with minimum sore of 50 as per CUI policy.
Career Advancement:
CU MBA programs offer inspiration, support and practical means for participants to achieve their goals whether they are seeking management level positions well reputed organizations, planning to start a new business or thinking about career progression. Graduates go on to find employment in a wide variety of roles, sectors and locations such as banking, telecommunications, health sector and many government and non-government sector organizations. Examples of career progression of successful MBA graduates could include taking up MTO and Executive level positions, or promotion from shipping manager to supply chain strategist, and from accounts assistant to financial services consultant. Graduates also take up Entrepreneurial roles.
How to apply
Click here
for information on how to apply

Master of Science in Mathematics

Graduate
Master of Science in Mathematics
Master of Science in Mathematics
Mission Statement
This programme is designed to prepare the students for research in both pure and applied mathematics. The department aims to chase quality in mathematics by providing an environment contributing to teaching, learning and research. It will also prepare the students to enhance its understanding by involving actively in research trends and applications in emerging fields.
Program Objective
Impart quality education to uunderstand basic insights and methods in a variety of mathematical areas
To prepare students for professional career in education and research institutions.
Synthesize formal theory into a comprehensive picture of phenomena.
Expose students to the global Mathematical Research environment both in pure and applied Mathematics.

PhD in Computer Science
Home
Doctoral
PhD in Computer Science
PhD Computer Science
Introduction
The aim of the PhD Computer Science program is to produce well trained scientists and researchers who can contribute both in academia and research. The curriculum of the program is designed by experts in various domains covering theoretical foundation with the latest technologies. Various stages of the degree program enable the students to get latest research ideas along with the theoretical background. The program enables the students to solve real world problems, contribute to scientific knowledge as well as the economy of the country. Research groups in different areas under the supervision of highly qualified faculty are working in the department. The areas of specialization include Natural Language Processing, Data Mining, Machine Learning, Artificial Intelligence, Networking, Coud Computing, and Image Processing.
Research Groups
Following research groups are actively working in the department.
PRiDE (Pattern Recognition, images & Data Engineering) Research Group
The Pattern Recognition, images and Data Engineering (PRiDE), founded by Dr. Khalid Iqbal, is part of the Department of Computer Science at the COMSATS University Islamabad, Attock Campus. The research group has been working on a wide range of research fields such as information retrieval, deep learning, Machine learning, Data Mining and Natural Language Processing. PRiDE is an integrated group of experts in diverse fields to transform imaginations into action.
InnoCloudX Research Group: Pioneering Distributed and Cloud Computing Innovations
Our Motto: Empowering Tomorrow’s Digital World Through Multidisciplinary Excellence
People:
Faculty Members
Muhammad Tahir Associate Professor (Tenured)
Muhammad Sardaraz Associate Professor (Tenured)
Scholars:
Sana Laraib (PhD Scholar)
Kamran (PhD Scholar)
Mehreen Safdar (MS Student)
Muneeba Rubab (MS Student)
Asad Ur Rehman (MS Student)
Overview:
InnoCloudX Research Group is at the forefront of cutting-edge research in the field of Distributed and Cloud Computing. Nestled at the intersection of cutting-edge technologies, our group thrives on innovation, collaboration, and the pursuit of knowledge in an ever-evolving digital landscape. Our multidisciplinary team is dedicated to advancing the frontiers of technology in areas such as Big Data Analytics, IoT, Blockchain, and Data Security. Leveraging the power of Machine Learning and AI, we are committed to developing innovative solutions that shape the future of computing and data management. With a passion for excellence and a mission to drive technological evolution, InnoCloudX Research Group is where visionary ideas become reality. Join us in redefining the possibilities of Distributed and Cloud Computing.
Mission:
Our mission is to harness the power of Distributed and Cloud Computing to reshape the future of technology. We are committed to pushing boundaries, fostering interdisciplinary collaboration, and solving real-world challenges through groundbreaking research. Our research group thrives on addressing complex challenges and delivering practical solutions that transform industries and drive technological progress.
Research Domains:
Big Data:
InnoCloudX explores the vast potential of Big Data analytics. We develop state-of-the-art algorithms and frameworks to process, analyze, and extract valuable insights from massive datasets. Our research empowers businesses to make data-driven decisions.
IoT (Internet of Things)
: Our research group pioneers advancements in IoT by designing scalable architectures and protocols, enabling seamless connectivity and data exchange among interconnected devices. Our innovators specialize in seamlessly integrating the IoT with cloud computing, enabling real-time data processing and control for smart devices and systems.
Blockchain
: In the realm of blockchain technology, InnoCloudX focuses on improving scalability, security, and consensus mechanisms. Our experts explore the potential of blockchain technology for secure and transparent data storage and transactions. We create novel applications of blockchain in various domains, including finance, healthcare, and supply chain.
Data Security
: Protecting data in the cloud is our top priority. We develop robust encryption and authentication methods, ensuring the confidentiality and integrity of sensitive information. Moreover, in an era of increasing cyber threats, our group is dedicated to enhancing data and information security using intrusion detection mechanisms.
Machine Learning and AI:
Our research leverages the power of Machine Learning and Artificial Intelligence to automate tasks, optimize processes, and enhance decision-making across a wide range of applications.
Approach:
At InnoCloudX Research Group, we believe in a holistic, multidisciplinary approach to research. We encourage cross-pollination of ideas and expertise, fostering collaboration between experts from diverse backgrounds to drive innovation.
Key Focus Areas:
Interdisciplinary Collaboration
:
We bring together experts from various domains to tackle complex problems, ensuring a well-rounded perspective.
Innovation
:
Innovation is at the core of our endeavors. We actively seek new and unconventional solutions to prevailing challenges.
Real-World Impact
:
Our research is grounded in practical applications. We aim to create technologies that improve lives and industries.
Ethical Considerations
:
We prioritize ethical considerations in all our research, ensuring that our innovations benefit society while respecting privacy and security.
Impact:
InnoCloudX Research Group’s work has the potential to transform industries and drive technological advancements. Our research output influences sectors such as finance, healthcare, logistics, and more, making a significant impact on the global digital landscape.
Why Choose InnoCloudX Innovators?
Multidisciplinary Excellence:
Our team comprises experts from diverse backgrounds, fostering creativity and innovation at the crossroads of multiple fields.
Cutting-Edge Research:
We stay at the forefront of technology, constantly pushing boundaries and exploring new horizons in cloud computing.
Practical Solutions:
InnoCloudX Innovators is dedicated to delivering real-world solutions that can be implemented to address the challenges of today and tomorrow.
Collaboration and Partnerships:
We actively seek collaborations with industry partners, academic institutions, and research organizations to accelerate the adoption of our innovations.
Join Us:
Are you passionate about the future of Distributed and Cloud Computing? InnoCloudX welcomes collaboration, partnerships, and talents who share our vision. Together, we can shape a smarter, more connected, and secure world through research and innovation.
Join us at InnoCloudX Research Group and be part of the journey towards a brighter digital future. Together, we innovate, collaborate, and make a difference.
Eligibility Criteria
An MS/M.Phil degree with thesis of 06 credit hours or its equivalent degree with thesis of 06 credit hours, in the relevant field from an accredited educational institution, with minimum CGPA of 3.0 / 4.0 (semester system) or 70 % marks (annual system.
No third division (annual system) or “D” grade (semester system) throughout the academic career.
GRE (subject) as per HEC policy or NTS GAT (subject) with minimum score of 60.
Schem of Studies.
:: CUOnline – Reports :: (comsats.edu.pk)

PhD in Electrical Engineering
Home
Doctoral
PhD in Electrical Engineering
Doctor of Philosophy (PhD) in Electrical Engineering
Program Overview
With new innovations emerging every day, pursuing a PhD in Electrical Engineering can open doors to diverse opportunities in this exciting field. The PhD Electrical Engineering Program at EE Department offers students opportunities to work on cutting-edge research projects, gain experience of addressing real-world problems in their research and develop a professional network at national as well as international level that prepares them for global careers. Graduate of this program are well-equipped to pursue a variety of career paths in related fields both in Pakistan and around the world.
The primary objective of our graduate programs is to impart education and training to a student in interest for pursuing graduate studies, to inculcate the spirit of learning in the student, and enhance his/her research orientation, critical thinking, research analysis capabilities, hypothesis testing and report writing skills.
Research Opportunities
Wireless communication and networks
Signal processing and image processing
Power and energy
RF design
Power electronics
Electrical machines
PhD Program Structure
A PhD scholar shall be required to complete 18 credit hours of graduate level course work. However, the scholar may be given exemption of up to two courses by the Board of Advanced Studies and Research (BASAR) on the recommendation of the scholar’s supervisory committee.
The scholar can register a minimum of 03 credit hours and maximum of 12 credit hours in a semester at PhD level.
The scholar can register an alternate elective course from the approved list of elective courses of the program in case the failed elective course is not being offered by the respective department.
The registration of PhD thesis of 09 credit hours will be after the completion of coursework of PhD.
Admission Criteria
For PhD
An MS/MPhil with Thesis/research project or its equivalent degree with Thesis/research project in the relevant field from an accredited educational institution with minimum CGPA of 3.0/4.0 under semester system or 70% under conventional system with no third division or D grade throughout the academic career.
GRE (subject) as per HEC policy, or GAT (subject) with at least 60% marks.
For admission in PhD Electrical Engineering Program, any one of the existing GAT (subject) tests in Electrical, Telecom or Electronics Engineering will be acceptable with a minimum score of 60% marks.
Curriculum
Students are required to register and pass 06 graduate level courses as mentioned in the scheme of studies and successfully defend their thesis.
https://cuonline.comsats.edu.pk/publicaccess/rptSearchCourseCatalogPA.aspx
Contact Information
Program Coordinator: Mr. Fayaz Ali,
Office Landline: +92-57-9316330
Ext: 241

PhD in Computer Engineering
Home
Doctoral
PhD in Computer Engineering
Doctor of Philosophy (PhD) in Computer Engineering
Program Overview
The world is rapidly progressing and technology has become an essential part of our lives. Computer Engineering is a field that plays a crucial role in shaping the technology of today and tomorrow. With new innovation emerging every day, pursuing a PhD in Computer Engineering can open doors to a plethora of opportunities in this exciting field. The PhD Computer Engineering of the ECE Department offers a comprehensive and advance program in Computer Engineering. With the strong focus on industry collaboration, the Computer Engineering program at ECE Department offers students opportunities to work on cutting-edge research projects, gain experience of addressing the real-world problems in their research and develop a professional network at national as well as international level that expose them to the global careers. Graduate of this program are well-equipped to pursue a variety of career paths in related fields both in Pakistan and around the world.
The primary objective of our graduate programs is to impart education and training to a student in the area of interest for pursuing graduate studies, to inculcate the spirit of learning in the student, and enhance his/her research orientation, critical thinking, research analysis capabilities, hypothesis testing and report writing skills.
Research Focus
IoT
Embedded Systems
Wireless Sensor Networks
Big Data
Multi- Agent Systems
Machine Learning
Computer Vision
Adhoc Vehicular Networks
Industrial Automation
RF Sensing
Advances in Biomedical
Curriculum
Students are required to register and pass 06 graduate level courses as mentioned in the scheme of studies and successfully defend their thesis.
Click Here for Scheme of Studies
in PhD Computer Engineering
Career Opportunities
Most of our graduates are working in academia. Some of the graduates go abroad for post-doctorate. Some of the graduates are working in industry.
Ph.D. Eligibility Criteria
MS/M.Phil. degree in the relevant field from an accredited educational institution
Minimum CGPA of 3 out of 4 (semester system) OR 70% marks (annual system)
No 3rd division throughout the academic career
NTS GAT Subject test minimum score of 60

PhD in Management Science
Home
Doctoral
PhD in Management Science
Ph.D. Management Science
Program Overview
The Department of Management Sciences at CUI Attock aims to provide a PhD program, which is both educationally sound and directly relevant to those areas of industry, commerce, public service, which Management Sciences graduates tend to enter. In developing the program, the Department has recognized that students may want to improve their job opportunities in academia or consultancy, change career direction or seek a fresh intellectual stimulus. PhD Management Sciences is being offered in the following areas of specialization:
Management/HRM
Finance
Marketing
Following are the salient features of the programme.
Salient features
Rigorous progarmme focused on adding to the existing body of knowledge
Has practical relevance for solving industry issues and problem
PhD management is focused on developing research skills
The programme would prepare students to publish in high quality journals
Eligibility Criteria
MS/M. Phil or equivalent degree in the relevant field from accredited institution with CGPA 3.0/4.0 or 70% marks with no third division (or D grade) throughout academic career.
NTS (subject) test with 60% marks
Programme Objectives
To develop understanding of existing body of knowledge of management
To develop research skills to solve industry problems
After the programme, students should be able to publish in high quality journals.
Program Structure
Category
Number of Courses

Career prospects / Opportunities
The PhD program prepares students for teaching and consultancy careers.
Teaching Methodology
Methods of teaching include, but are not limited to:
Lectures
Case studies
Class discussions
Group studies
Assignments
Quizzes
This methodology enables students to develop the following transferable and intellectual skills by integrating them in the curriculum of different offered courses:
Conceptual skills
Human skills
Technical skills (subject related know-how)
Analytical skills
Reading/Writing Skills
Computer Skills
Communication Skills
Listening skills
Research Skills

PhD in Mathematics
Home
Doctoral
PhD in Mathematics
PhD in Mathematics
The department of Mathematics CUI Attock Campus is enriched with highly qualified faculty with a firm commitment to academic prowess. The faculty is dedicated to an unwavering pursuit of excellence in elevating the standards of mathematical education. The department offers PhD Mathematics in diverse fields of research in pure and applied Mathematics that serves as a beacon of inspiration for research productivity throughout the region. We proudly hold the distinction of being the pioneering and sole institution in the Attock district to offer this esteemed degree program.
Research Areas:
Mathematical Inequalities and Applications
Numerical Analysis
Commutative Algebra
Fluid Mechanics
Mathematical Analysis
Elastodynamics
Mathematical Biology
Graph Theory
Fixed Point Theory
Functional Analysis
Probability Theory and Mathematical Statistics
Survey Sampling and Time Series Analysis
Computing Facilities:
Mathematica
Python
MatLab
Maple
Scientific Work Place
SAS
R Language
EView

Library
Home
Library
Check out our books
The Library at CUI Attock campus is spacious well planned and provides a calm and peaceful environment. It is rapidly developing into one of the richest information resource centers in Attock. The library subscribes to a wide range of periodicals and journals that are valuable for students academic needs. It also provides a strong learning atmosphere supported by electronic information access and modern services.
The library includes circulation reserve and reference sections. Internet facilities allow users to connect with libraries around the world for reference assistance and consultation. The library is fully equipped with a modern audiovisual system. Students are encouraged to use educational materials available on videotapes CDs DVDs and audiotapes. Resources can be searched through a state of the art computerized library catalogue system.
A dedicated silence area provides students with an ideal environment for focused study. The library resources and services are mainly intended for faculty members and students but they are also accessible to employees of all departments and faculties.

Digital Library
The CUI Attock Library is a regular user of the HEC Digital Library. The Library user can access more than 30,000 online Journals / Magazines. HEC Digital Library offers the following links to access the digital resources.
ACM

Accessibility of Digital Resources
Above mentioned database can be accessed through live IPs and VPN, so the library user can access their required information through any terminal which exist in the campus premises or get access from home through VPN. Apart from the academic blocks, The
WIFI facility
for the laptop users also available in the campus, so, the users having laptops can use Digital Library from any point of the Campus

Book Fairs / Exhibitions
Apart from our day to day book acquisition the library also arrange the Book Fairs / Exhibitions to acquire the books for the library.
The main idea of said Fairs / Exhibition is to develop reading habits and create interest of readings among students and faculty. The second purpose of this exhibition is to create awareness regarding the leading major book companies and their products such as Books, Journals CDs, etc.
The well reputed venders from through out the country participated in said Fair / Exhibitions with latest collection of books particular on other subject areas.
Faculty and students not only recommends the books for the library but also purchased on special discount from the venders.
Services
The CUI Attock Library proudly presents the following services to its users:
Circulation of Books
Online Renewal
Online Reservation
Reference Services
Library Book Procurement
Library Material Searching Facility
Inter Library Loan
Current Awareness Services (CAS)
Selective Dissemination of Information services (SDI) (Only for Researchers)
Newspapers Clipping Services
Internet Search via latest computers
Wireless router facility for laptop users
Virtual Private Connection Facility
Similarity Index Report
Wi-Fi facility
Inside  COMSATS Attock Library
Our expert librarians and archivists support students, faculty, staff, and the public through vast archives and cutting-edge technologies.

Campus Life
Our thriving residential campus is home to a community of creative and accomplished people from around the world.
Student Life
Student Affairs
Promoting student wellbeing through support services leadership development and a vibrant campus experience.

Structures & Buildings

A serene place for prayer and reflection fostering spiritual growth unity and peaceful campus life.

The Research Enterprise
Innovation & Collaboration
Innovation emerges when different fields intersect and creative minds collaborate to discover new solutions together.
Ideas & Discovery
New ideas are born when different disciplines connect and researchers explore uncharted possibilities.
Knowledge & Breakthroughs
Breakthroughs occur at the crossroads of knowledge where collaboration sparks inventive solutions.
Students Start-Up Business Center (SSBC)
COMSATS University Islamabad, Attock Campus actively promotes a culture of entrepreneurship and innovation through structured academic, research, and mentorship initiatives. The university fosters student innovation and entrepreneurial talent by strengthening university industry collaboration and providing platforms for applied learning and startup development.
As part of this commitment, the campus has established the
Students Start Up Business Center (SSBC)
to support student led startups through continuous mentorship capacity building programs professional training and strong industry linkages. The Center engages experts from academia industry banking technology public policy and entrepreneurship to guide students in areas such as startups leadership artificial intelligence fintech sustainability and agri-preneurship.
Students are regularly encouraged to develop and present innovative business ideas through structured pitching forums and evaluation by expert panels. Dedicated startup workspaces prototype development facilities and display platforms further enhance experiential learning collaboration and networking. Outstanding ideas and impactful startups are recognized through merit-based awards promoting innovation social impact and entrepreneurial excellence.

Scholarships & Financial Aid
Home
Scholarships
Scholarships & Financial Aid
At COMSATS University Attock University, we are committed to supporting academic excellence and ensuring that deserving students have access to quality education. Through a range of scholarship opportunities, we aim to recognize and reward outstanding achievements. Explore the various scholarships available:
Scholarships
Admission Merit Topper Scholarship
Description:
This reward is dedicated to recognizing academic excellence at the very start of the university journey. It is awarded to the students who top the admission merit list of each program.
Benefit:
Full tuition fee covered.
Eligibility
:
Student who top the admission merit list of any program will be awarded admission merit topper scholarship.
Balochistan Education Endowment Fund (BEEF)
Description:
In collaboration with the Government of Balochistan, this scholarship supports students having Balochistan local/domicile to pursue higher education at CUI Attock.
Benefit:
Full Fee Coverage.
Eligibility
:
Students must possess a Balochistan domicile and maintain a minimum CGPA as per BEEF policy.
Benazir Undergraduate Scholarship Project (BUSP)
Description:
Formerly known as the Ehsaas Scholarship, BUSP is a flagship initiative of the Government of Pakistan to support students from low-income families.
Benefit:
Full fee coverage along with semester wise stipend.
Eligibility
:
Underprivileged students with low income enrolled in undergraduate programs.
Daanish Schools Scholars
Description:
CUI Attock signed an MoU with Danish Authority and PEEF to facilitate their students. Danish Schools recommends the students for onward concession as per MoU.
Benefit:
Financial assistance as per the MoU between CUI and Daanish Schools.
Eligibility
:
Must be a confirmed graduate of a Daanish School with a strong academic record.
Full Fee Waiver Scheme for Disabled Persons
Description:
CUI Attock is committed to inclusivity. This scheme ensures that students with physical or sensory disabilities have equal access to education without financial burden.
Benefit:
100% fee waiver.
Eligibility
:
Valid disability certificate issued by the relevant government authority (Social Welfare Department).
Diya Pakistan Scholarship
Description:
Diya Pakistan is a reputable philanthropic organization providing merit-cum-need-based stipends to talented students.
Benefit:
Partial financial stipend to cover academic costs.
Eligibility
:
Students with at least 60% marks in previous exams and a verifiable financial need.
Ehsaan Trust (Interest-Free Loan)
Description:
In partnership with Ehsaan Trust (Meezan Bank), CUI Attock offers a “Qarz-e-Hasna” (interest-free loan) facility for students facing temporary financial hardships.
Benefit:
Interest-free loan for tuition fees, repayable in easy installments.
Eligibility
:
Purely need-based, subject to an interview and financial assessment.
Employees Pecuniary Assistance
Description:
To honor the dedication of the COMSATS workforce, this assistance is provided to the children of CUI employees.
Benefit:
Full tuition fee coverage.
Eligibility
:
Children’s of CUI employees are eligible.
Honhar Scholarship Program
Description:
A flagship initiative of the Government of Punjab aimed at providing high-quality education to the brightest minds of the province.
Benefit:
Comprehensive coverage of educational expenses for the duration of the degree.
Eligibility
:
Residents of Punjab meeting the specific merit and income criteria set by the Punjab Higher Education Commission (PHEC).
PAC Kamra Wards Fee Concession
Description:
Under a special MoU, children of Pakistan Aeronautical Complex (PAC) Kamra employees are eligible for financial concessions at the Attock Campus.
Benefit:
Fixed percentage reduction in tuition fees.
Eligibility
:
Recommended students from PAC as per MoU will be awarded PAC wards fee concession.
Merit Scholarship (CUI Internal)
Description:
This scholarship is awarded every semester to students who demonstrate exceptional academic performance during their stay at CUI.
Benefit:
A concession of Rs 20,000, 30,000 and 50,000 will be awarded to students who achieve excellent CGPA range (as per merit scholarship policy) during the study. This is also applicable for the new intakes.
PEEF Scholarship
Description:
The Punjab Education Endowment Fund (PEEF) provides opportunities for talented and deserving students of Punjab to complete their university education.
Benefit:
Monthly stipends and/or tuition fee coverage.
Eligibility
:
Students with Punjab domicile who have passed their intermediate exams from a government institution and meet the income criteria.

CU-Online
Home
CU-Online
Overview
To provide a one-stop solution for addressing the needs of departmental heads, faculty members, and students, CUI Islamabad Campus has implemented a university management system called CU-Online. CU-Online is a platform that offers consolidated academic services to both faculty and students.
Administrative Services
Departmental heads and program coordinators have access to CU-Online, which provides consolidated performance insights for students enrolled in their respective departments. All student related matters are integrated into CU-Online to offer a comprehensive view of overall academic performance, both at the individual and collective levels.
Faculty Services
All faculty members have access to CU-Online according to their allocated courses, where they can upload course materials such as lectures, assignments, and quizzes. In addition, CU-Online includes a result management console that calculates semester results and grades based on marks obtained under different assessment criteria.
Student Services
Students can access all course materials through CU-Online. The services provided to students via CU-Online include:
Lecture Details
Attendance Records
Course Registration
Progress Reports
Fee Status
Parental Console

Message From The Rector
Home
Rector
Message From The Rector
by
December 20, 2025
Rector
Dear Students, Faculty Members, and Visitors.
It gives me great pleasure to welcome you to
COMSATS University Islamabad (CUI), Attock Campus
an integral part of a vibrant multi campus university system committed to academic excellence innovation and national development.
Over the years COMSATS University Islamabad has established itself as a leading institution of higher learning in Pakistan with a strong reputation for quality education impactful research and ethical values. The Attock Campus proudly contributes to this vision by providing a dynamic academic environment where knowledge creativity and professional competence are nurtured.
At CUI we firmly believe that universities play a transformative role in shaping societies. Our focus extends beyond imparting academic knowledge to developing critical thinking problem solving abilities and a sense of social responsibility among our students. Through modern curricula innovative teaching methodologies and a culture of research we strive to prepare graduates who can meet the challenges of a rapidly changing world and the demands of the Fourth Industrial Revolution.
The Attock Campus offers a supportive and intellectually stimulating atmosphere where students and faculty work together in the pursuit of learning and discovery. Emphasis is placed on both academic rigor and personal development ensuring that our graduates are not only technically proficient but also confident ethical and ready to contribute positively to society.
As you explore this website I hope you gain valuable insight into our academic programs campus facilities and the opportunities available at CUI Attock. Whether you are a prospective student, a member of the academic community or a visitor I encourage you to engage with us and become part of the COMSATS legacy of excellence.
I am confident that with dedication collaboration and the guidance of our capable faculty and administration the Attock Campus will continue to grow and make meaningful contributions to education and research in the region.
I pray to Almighty Allah for continued success and guidance in our collective efforts and look forward to the achievements that lie ahead.
Prof. Dr. Raheel Qamar
(
T.I
)

Message by the Director
Home
Director
Message by the Director
by
December 20, 2025
Director
COMSATS University Islamabad, Attock Campus.
It is a matter of great honor and pleasure for me to welcome students faculty members parents and visitors to COMSATS University Islamabad Attock Campus. Our campus stands as a vibrant center of learning innovation and personal growth within the larger COMSATS University system.
I am deeply grateful to the Worthy Rector
Prof. Dr. Raheel Qamar (T.I)
for giving me the opportunity to serve COMSATS University Islamabad, Attock Campus and contribute to its academic and institutional progress.
CUI Attock Campus is committed to providing quality education that combines academic excellence practical knowledge and strong ethical values. We strive to create an environment where students are encouraged to think independently develop professional competence and prepare themselves to contribute positively to society.
Our academic programs are designed to meet modern educational and industry requirements. Emphasis is placed on teaching research innovation and skill development so that our graduates are ready to face the challenges of a rapidly evolving world. Along with academic pursuits we strongly support co curricular activities that help students build confidence leadership and teamwork.
The campus continues to grow with the support and vision of the Principal Seat and the guidance of the Worthy Rector. Dedicated faculty members supportive staff and enthusiastic students collectively contribute to the progress and success of this campus.
I warmly welcome the newly admitted students and wish them a rewarding academic journey. I also extend my best wishes to our continuing students and encourage them to pursue their goals with dedication and integrity. I invite parents and visitors to explore the campus and share in our commitment to excellence.
May Allah guide us in our efforts and grant us continued success in serving education and the nation.
Prof. Dr. Nadia Nawaz Qadri
Director
COMSATS University Islamabad Attock Campus

Bachelor of Science in Software Engineering
Home
Undergraduate
Bachelor of Science in Software Engineering
Bachelor of Science in Software Engineering BS(SE)
Program Overview
BS Software Engineering is designed to prepare students for careers in software engineering, software project management, and software development and integration. This outcome includes developing technical competency as well as leadership and communication skills necessary to analyze, design, verify, validate, implement, and maintain software systems. CUI software engineers learn how to apply the principles of computer science, engineering, and analysis to the design, creation, testing, and evaluation of software and digital systems.
Software Engineering covers a wide spectrum of areas within the field of software engineering, ranging from the theoretical to practical. A software engineer can specialize in areas such as software engineering, requirement engineering, quality engineering, software testing and project management.
It is a four years program consisting of eight semesters. The maximum duration for completion of this degree is twelve semesters. The degree is awarded on completion of minimum 133 credit hours, including six credits for the project, with a passing CGPA of at least 2.0/4.0.
Students will be able to successfully:
Develop software requirements and functional specifications
Use proven techniques to design software structure before it is implemented
Apply established verification and validation techniques
Understand the importance of constructing large software systems using standardized components and reusing existing code (modules) where possible
Use software tools as effective aids in all phases of software development
Design, develop and deliver software in a cost-effective manner
Understand new technologies
Career Outcomes
The Bachelor of Software Engineering is concerned with the design, construction, operation and maintenance of software systems. This course provides students with the technical expertise to design and construct software, and management skills needed to plan and operate complex software systems. Students will gain skills and become capable of creating stand-alone, mobile, networked, and web based software solutions for a range of different domains. Software Engineering graduate has the option to work in many different sectors such as software industry, telecommunications, finance, health care, manufacturing, retailing, security, transport, etc. Other engineering areas like aeronautical, automotive, building, electrical, etc. also have increasing needs for software engineering. The entertainment industry with video games and movie animation too has a large demand for Software Engineers. In addition the SE program develops a strong background for pursuing higher education and research.
Eligibility
Students are eligible for admission if they have Intermediate or equivalent
(‘A’ Level)
with minimum 50% marks from accredited institution and
*NTS-NAT
test score with minimum 50% marks.
* Detailed information can be obtained from
http://www.nts.org.pk

Bachelor of Science in Artificial Intelligence
Home
Undergraduate
Bachelor of Science in Artificial Intelligence
Bachelors in Artificial Intelligence
Program Overview
Artificial Intelligence technology mimics human thinking by learning from past experiences and recognizing patterns. AI technologies have revolutionized the way we live and work. They can now seamlessly perform complex tasks such as identifying objects, recognizing speech, translating languages, detecting faces, and analyzing sentiments. With such capabilities, AI has the power to transform industries and improve our quality of life. Artificial intelligence is not just limited to well-known personal assistants like Siri, Google Now, or IBM’s Watson. In fact, it is pervasive in our lives. Recent advancements in the field of neural networks have enabled scientists to make significant strides in replicating the processes of actual neurons. This progress has coincided with an exponential increase in data, which experts now consider as valuable as oil. The development of deep learning has empowered machines to process information at a sophisticated level, allowing them to perform complex functions such as facial recognition and next-generation genome sequencing.
The Attock Campus of COMSATS University recognizes the importance of AI in today’s world and its potential to drive significant progress in the region. With this in mind, the university has launched a cutting-edge undergraduate program in Artificial Intelligence, aimed at providing students with a comprehensive understanding of the field and the skills they need to succeed in a rapidly evolving job market. The program is led by a team of highly talented faculty members who are dedicated to helping students develop their analytical and computational abilities through real-world projects and hands-on experience. By focusing on problem-solving, innovation, and critical thinking, the program aims to equip students with the technical and transferable skills that are essential for a successful career in AI. The curriculum has been designed to meet the specific requirements of the industry, as well as the accreditation guidelines set forth by the NCEAC. Through this program, students can expect to gain a deep understanding of the latest AI technologies and their practical applications, and emerge as well-rounded professionals ready to make a meaningful impact in the field of Artificial Intelligence.
The bachelor’s in artificial intelligence is a 4-year degree program and consists of 130 credit hours. The core computer science courses covered in this program include Programming Fundamentals, Object Oriented Programming, Data Structures and Algorithms, Operating Systems, Digital Logic Design, Database Systems, Computer Networks, and Software Engineering Concepts. The artificial intelligence courses covered in the degree include Introduction of Artificial Intelligence, Machine Learning, Data Mining, Deep Learning, Computer Vision, Natural Language Processing, Robotics, Experts Systems, and Pattern Recognition.
Program Mission
We are committed to delivering exceptional artificial intelligence education, innovative research, and expert professional services to promote the socio-economic progress of the community. Through our programs, we aim to equip students with the knowledge, skills, and hands-on experience they need to excel in AI-related careers and make meaningful contributions to society. Our unwavering dedication to excellence and lifelong learning ensures that our graduates remain at the forefront of this rapidly evolving field.
Program Educational Objectives (PEOs)
Our Program Education Objectives state that within a few years of graduation:
Students are expected to have a comprehensive understanding of artificial intelligence, including intelligent perception and design.
Students should possess strong skills in engineering and scientific research, as well as creativity, hands-on abilities, and communication and leadership skills.
Students should possess strong moral, cultural, and ethical values, as well as a sense of responsibility and physical fitness.
Students are expected to possess strong cognitive abilities, resilience, effective communication skills, good mental health, optimism, and proactivity.
Students Outcomes (SOs)
Understand and explain the fundamental concepts and theories of computer science and related fields.
Analyze a complex computing problem and apply principles of computing and other relevant disciplines to identify solutions.
Design, implement, and evaluate a computing-based solution to meet a given set of computing requirements in the context of the Program’s discipline.
Communicate effectively in a variety of professional contexts.
Recognize professional responsibilities and make informed judgments in computing practice based on legal and ethical principles.
Function effectively as a member or leader of a team engaged in activities appropriate to the program’s discipline.
Apply computer science theory and software development fundamentals to produce computing-based solutions.
Apply Artificial Intelligence principles and techniques for problem solving and decision making.
Career Opportunities
AI software engineering
Machine learning system developer.
Data mining expert
AI Data scientist.
Knowledge engineering expert
AI data analytics expert
AI in logistic and supply chain expert
AI in e-commerce expert
AI Research engineer
Admission Requirements
The eligibility criteria for candidates applying for admission to the
BSAI
program are listed below:
Intermediate or equivalent
(‘A’ Level)
with minimum 50% marks from accredited institution.
*NTS-NAT
test score with minimum 50% marks.

The Laptop Distribution Ceremony
Home
All Campus
The Laptop Distribution Ceremony
by
January 28, 2026
A proud day at COMSATS University Islamabad, Attock Campus.
The Laptop Distribution Ceremony was held to celebrate merit and support academic excellence, where *178 deserving students* were awarded laptops under the PM Laptop Scheme.
We were honored to have *Prof. Dr. Nadia Nawaz, Director CUI Attock Campus, as the Chief Guest. The ceremony was also graced by **Mr. Rana Tahir Mehmood, Senior Manager, and **Ms. Ghazala Naz, APO*, from the Registrar Office, Principal Seat.
The session was supervised by *Khawaja Muhammad Ali Butt, Deputy Registrar / Manager SFAO, CUI Attock Campus*, who also shared a concise overview of the performance and contributions of the Students Financial Aid Office since its inception.
Congratulations to all the recipients. May these laptops support your learning, research, and future success.
2 Janvary 2026
.
