PEEF Masters Level Scholarship Quota (Fall 2025 & Spring 2026)
Home
All Campus
PEEF Masters Level Scholarship Quota (Fall 2025 & Spring 2026)
by
January 28, 2026
Punjab Educational Endowment Fund (PEEF) announced Master’s Level Scholarships for Academic Year 2025-26 (
Fall – 2025 and Spring – 2026 Intakes Only
).
These scholarships will be offered to students fulfilling the criteria given below:
Punjab domicile.
Secured at least 60% marks or a minimum CGPA 2.5 in graduation level examination held in 2023-24, 2024-25, 2025-26 (fall/spring sessions) from Punjab (minimum sixteen years of schooling or 4-year education after HSSC / F.A / F. Sc / Grade 12 examination).
Secured admission as a full-time student in the current academic year (2025-26) in one of the partner universities/degree-awarding institutions.
Students enrolled in fall/spring sessions (where applicable) and morning/ afternoon/ evening sessions (where applicable) are eligible to apply for the PEEF Master’s level scholarship.
Declared monthly income of parents (from all sources) is equal to or less than sixty thousand (Rs. 60,000/-).
Children of Govt. employees in BPS 1-4 are exempted from condition of monthly income, if salary is the only source of income
Children of civilians martyred in terrorist attacks are exempted from condition of monthly income.
Not availing any other educational scholarship during the current academic year.
Students who have already passed/ possessed MA/ MSc. / MS/ MPhil. etc. Degrees are
Ineligible
to apply for PEEF Master Level Scholarship.
Deadline to apply:
1st March 2026.

Pakistan Petroleum Limited (PPL) Scholarship for FY 2025-26
Home
All Campus
Pakistan Petroleum Limited (PPL) Scholarship for FY 2025-26
by
January 28, 2026
Pakistan Petroleum Limited (PPL)
hasannounced the
Higher Professional Education Scholarship Program (FY 2025–26)
for students at public sector universities.
The scholarship is available for students studying in the fields of
Engineering, Medicine, Information Technology, Business Administration, and Education
, and is aimed at promoting higher education in operational districts across Pakistan.
This scholarship program is specifically dedicated to students belonging to the following districts:
Matyari, Sanghar, Kashmore, Chakwal, Tehsil Gujar Khan of Rawalpindi, UC Chhab, Dakhnair & Tehsil Jhand of District Attock
.
A total of
42 scholarships
are being offered, including
2 scholarships reserved for female students
from the mentioned operational areas.
Eligibility Criteria :
Bonafide resident of the respective district
Minimum 60% marks in the last examination
Enrolled in the 1st year / first and second semester or early stages of Bachelor’s/Master’s degree at an HEC-recognized public sector institution
Age not more than 28 years
Not receiving any other scholarship
Demonstrated financial need
The scholarship is awarded for
(01) year
, extendable up to
(04)/(05) years
based on academic performance and availability of funds.
Students can apply online through the PPL website:
http://www.ppl.com.pk/content/education/scholarship-schemes
The
l
ast date to apply is
January 11, 2026
.
Queries:
ScholarshipSchemes@ppl.com.pk
Deadline to apply:
January 11, 2026

25th Year of Excellence Silver Jubilee Celebration 2025
Home

All Campus
25th Year of Excellence Silver Jubilee Celebration 2025
About The Event
25 Years. One Legacy. One Celebration.
COMSATS University Islamabad proudly marks its Silver Jubilee, celebrating 25 years of excellence in knowledge, leadership, and lasting impact.
A look back at the Silver Jubilee Celebrations at CUI Attock held on 26th December 2025.
The event was graced by Chief Guest Prof. Dr. Nadia Nawaz Qadri, Director CUI Attock Campus, who addressed the gathering and shared her reflections with the audience.
CUI Attock Campus joins the entire COMSATS community in honoring this remarkable milestone with pride and gratitude.

Department of Computer Engineering
Home
About Us CE
About Us
With a vision to produce professional engineering graduates, the Department of Electrical Engineering was established in 2007. The EE department aims to achieve the academic and research excellence in the subject area through its well-designed curriculum, strong focus on research and innovation, objective based learning and strong industrial liaison. Moreover the department believes and strives to provide the excellent facilities, best teaching methods and learning environment to the students in order to achieve professional and academic excellence.
Since its inception in 2007, the Department of Electrical Engineering has successfully launched multiple degree programs, including BS (Electrical Engineering), MS (Electrical Engineering) and BS (Computer Engineering) in a short span of time. The curriculum of these programs encompasses the vast background of electrical and computer engineering. The EE department offers a wide range of elementary as well as advanced courses pertaining to the broad range of specializations including Electrical Power, Telecommunications, Electronics, Computer and Control Systems. In order to provide students with the research and internship opportunities, CUI has strong collaboration with Pakistan Aeronautical Complex (PAC) Kamra under a Memorandum of Understanding.
All engineering programs offered by the department are recognized by Pakistan Engineering Council (PEC) because of the excellent educational standards of CUI and commitment of the faculty.
The major objectives of department are summarized as:
To develop graduates with strong academic foundation in multiple areas of specialization.
To enhance the analytical and problem solving skills of graduates and induce critical thinking.
To inculcate a strong sense of ethics and professionalism in its graduates to make significant and positive contribution to the industry and society at large.

Academics Office
Home
Academics Office
Academics Office
Registrar Office-Academic Unit is headed by Khawaja Muhammad Ali Butt Deputy Registrar CUI Attock and is fully responsible for smooth conduct of academic activities. Academics Unit has been maintaining all type of students’ record (both soft and hard) Main functions are as under:
Services
Student Orientation, Registration, ID Card Issuance, Course Registration, Drop, Withdrawal, Freezing/Rejoining of Studies, Readmission, and Inter-Campus Migration.
Issuance of official certificates such as NOC, Medium of Instruction, Bonafide, etc., on student requests.
Fee Refund processing in accordance with university policy.
Custodian of the student master list and responsible for maintaining academic and administrative records in an organized manner.
Verification of academic documents of newly admitted students from relevant boards and universities.
Managing the academic and administrative matters of foreign students enrolled at CUI Attock Campus.
Preparing the Academic Calendar and compiling information for newsletters and various institutional reports.
Support
Providing continuous support to the Director Campus in all academic matters and facilitating the implementation of decisions made by University Authorities.
Assisting academic departments in correspondence and compliance matters with regulatory and accreditation bodies such as HEC, PEC, NBEAC, and NCEAC, etc.
Providing support to academic department in preparing and submitting proposals for the launch of new academic programs at CUI Attock Campus.
Providing operational and administrative support for hybrid learning modes and related academic initiatives.
Coordinating and managing litigation cases pertaining to academic and administrative matters of CUI Attock Campus.
Coordination and Legal Matters
Acting as the primary liaison with the Principal Seat and other relevant departments, streamlining communication and ensuring consistent implementation of institutional policies.
Spearheading the Hybrid Learning Program as the Focal Person, coordinating across departments to enhance blended learning opportunities and increase student engagement.
Managing legal matters for CUI Attock Campus, including handling contracts, resolving disputes, and ensuring compliance with national and institutional legal frameworks.
Team
Khawaja Muhammad Ali Butt

Financial Aid

Financial Aid
Financial Aid
Scholarship Unit is headed by Khawaja Muhammad Ali Butt, Deputy Registrar. Students’ Financial Aid Office at CUI Attock Campus was established on May 30, 2013 with the aim to
Liaison with CUI Principal Seat and Donor Agencies
Provide assistance to qualified students to obtain the financial aid they need to in achieving their educational goals
Help students and their parents search for, apply, receive and maintain eligibility for various types of financial aid.
Provide proactive and responsive financial aid counseling
Team

Student Affairs
Home
Student Affairs
Student Affairs
Student Affairs Office at CUI Attock facilitates students with solution to their routine problems/issues on campus. This office consists of Career Development Center and Student guidance and counseling. One window operations are carried out and a dedicated staff ensures that each and every query of students is addressed with satisfactory results. Career Development Center is endeavoring to enhance industry-academia linkage and explore multiple job opportunities for graduating students. CDC invites representatives from industry on a regular basis to have interaction with students. Apart from regular liaison with industry, it also conducts Job and Career fairs where top repute organizations are invited for selection of talented students.
Phone:
057- 9049158, 9049159
Email:
studentaffairsoffice@cuiatk.edu.pk

Extra Curricular
Extra Curricular
The ECA Office is running under the supervision of Dr. Faisal Shahzad, Assistant Professor, Management Sciences Department. This office is responsible for smooth conduction of semester- wise Sports and literary activities (indoor & outdoor) at CUI Attock Campus. There are also 12 student societies are operating under this office to provide the students a platform where they can get exposure of their co-curricular activities, and their abilities can be acknowledged for their personal growth as well as betterment of the organization.

Master of Science in Management Science
Home
Graduate
Master of Science in Management Science
Master of Science in Management Sciences MS(MS)
Mission Statement
The aim of MS program is to foster knowledge by conducting research within the domain of business/management sciences and producing socially responsible leaders. These leaders will not only help business organizations through research but also serve the community through their superior knowledge.
Program Objectives:
To produce socially responsible graduates
Creation and dissemination of knowledge through published research
To address the contemporary issues of organization in a systematic way
To enable graduates to work on various research projects independently
To enable graduates to work in diverse cultural environment
To enable graduates to serve the community through their superior knowledge

Master of Science in Project Management
Home
Graduate
Master of Science in Project Management
Master of Science in Project Management (MSPM)
Mission Statement
The main objective of providing education within this program of MS (PM) is to develop a workforce with specific skills of research and preparing complete feasibilities, planning, monitoring and evaluation of the projects to lead each project to a level of success beyond the targets on sustainable routine.
Objectives
Provide key education on project management portfolio
Develop key skills in research in project management
Develop key skills of managing projects
Develop key skills in latest technology for project management
Develop key skills in latest technology for project management

Bachelor of Science Business Data Analytics
Home
Undergraduate
Bachelor of Science Business Data Analytics
Bachelor of Science (Business Data Analytics) – BS (BDA)
Program Overview:
In today’s business landscape, data is often referred to as the ‘new oil,’ serving as the lifeblood of the digital economy. Businesses now recognize data as a critical asset, making the ability to identify opportunities within data an essential skill. How can vast amounts of information be harnessed to reveal key insights about business performance? How can trends be recognized, and opportunities interpreted using analytical tools? The Bachelor of Science in Business Data Analytics program at COMSATS University Islamabad, Attock Campus, offered by the Department of Management Sciences, prepares students to develop these high-demand skills crucial for success in the era of Industry 4.0.
The BS in Business Data Analytics is designed to equip students with the expertise to analyze and interpret data for informed business decision-making. The program emphasizes statistical techniques, data analysis, and data-driven strategies tailored to solve real-world business challenges. Students will gain the skills to collect, analyze, and interpret large datasets, providing valuable insights that support strategic decision-making.
Graduates of the Business Data Analytics program are well-prepared to operate at the intersection of data science and business strategy. Career paths include roles as business analysts, data analysts, market research analysts, and more. The four-year program features hands-on projects, internships, and research opportunities, ensuring graduates have practical experience in addition to theoretical knowledge.
Program Objectives
The BS Business Data Analytics program aims to:
Build Analytical Proficiency:
Develop students who can understand, apply, and effectively communicate the language, theories, and models of data science in a business context.
Problem-Solving Expertise:
Enable students to critically evaluate, synthesize, and solve complex structured and unstructured business problems using data-driven approaches.
Foster Innovation and Entrepreneurship:
Encourage an entrepreneurial mindset and a proactive approach toward business improvements and innovation.
Promote Ethical Decision-Making:
Instill a strong sense of ethics and social responsibility, ensuring that graduates contribute positively to their organizations and society.
Entry Requirements
To be eligible for admission, applicants must meet the following criteria:
Educational Qualification:
Intermediate or equivalent (‘A’ Level) with a minimum of 50% marks from an accredited institution.
Admission Test:
NTS-NAT test score with a minimum of 50% marks, in accordance with CUI policy.
Application Process:
Prospective students can apply online through (link to portal) and must submit soft copies of all required documents.
Program Structure
The BS BDA program requires 135 credit hours, completed over a minimum of eight semesters (4 years) and a maximum of twelve semesters (6 years). The curriculum includes:
Core Areas:
Business Data Analytics, Machine Learning, Financial Technology, HR Analytics, and Marketing Analytics.
Specializations:
Students can choose electives in:
Data Science and AI
Financial Analytics
HR and Talent Analytics
Marketing Analytics
Internship Requirement:
The program includes a mandatory
three-credit hour internship
, providing students with essential hands-on industry experience and the opportunity to apply their analytical skills in a real-world business environment.
Capstone Project:
In the final year, students are required to complete a
six-credit hour.
This project involves addressing a complex, real-world business challenge using advanced data analytics techniques, showcasing the student’s ability to apply program knowledge to practical scenarios.
Career Prospects
Graduates of the BS Business Data Analytics program are well-prepared for a variety of roles, including:
Entrepreneurship:
Encouraged to start their own businesses or data-driven ventures.
Employment Opportunities:
Job roles in multinationals, telecom industry, real estate, e-commerce, financial services, and consultancy firms as:
Data Analysts
Business Analysts
Market Research Analysts
Business Intelligence Specialists
Data Scientists
Admission and Eligibility Criteria
Program Intake
Sessions Offered:
The program is available in both Fall (September) and Spring (February) sessions.
Admission Requirements
Educational Qualification:
Applicants must have completed Intermediate or equivalent (‘A’ Level) with a minimum of 50% marks from an accredited institution.
Admission Test:
A valid NTS-NAT test score with a minimum of 50% marks is required as per CUI policy.
Program Duration
Minimum Duration:
8 semesters (4 years)
Maximum Duration:
12 semesters (6 years)
Required Documents for Admission
Applicants must submit the following documents along with the admission form:
Demand Draft
in favor of CUI Islamabad Campus from any bank.
Matric/O-Level Mark Sheet
& Equivalence Certificate (photocopy back to back).
FA/FSc/A-Level Mark Sheet
& Equivalence Certificate (photocopy back to back).
BA/B.Sc/B.Com/BBA (2 years)
Mark Sheet & Equivalence Certificate (for BBS applicants only).
Copy of NIC/B-Form
.
Valid NTS Result
(photocopy) if the test has already been taken.
Paid NTS Challan Form
(original copy) if the NTS test has not yet been taken.
Hope Certificate/Affidavit
(notarized on Rs. 20/- Stamp Paper) for result-awaiting applicants.
Undertaking
(notarized on Rs. 20/- Stamp Paper) for all applicants.
Academic Policies and Attendance
Attendance Requirement:
A minimum of 80% attendance is mandatory to be eligible for examinations.
Examination Rules:
Students must arrive on time for exams. Latecomers (beyond 30 minutes) will not be allowed to sit for the examination.
A valid Student ID Card and Admit Card are mandatory for all exams.
Prohibited Items: No written materials, scientific calculators, digital diaries, or mobile phones are allowed in the examination hall.
Penalties for Unfair Practices:
Fine up to Rs. 20,000/-
Cancellation of the entire examination result
Expulsion or rustication from the institute
Academic Structure and Regulations
Semester Duration:
Each semester consists of 15-18 weeks of teaching, excluding examinations. There are two regular semesters per academic year at CUI.
Credit Hours:
One credit hour corresponds to at least one hour of teaching per week throughout the semester.
A full-time student is one who is registered for at least 12 credit hours in a semester.
GPA and CGPA:
GPA (Grade Point Average):
The weighted average of grades earned in a semester.
CGPA (Cumulative Grade Point Average):
The weighted average of grades earned throughout the program.
Academic Standing and Course Management
Probation and Dismissal:
Students with a CGPA below 2.0 will be placed on academic probation.
If a student receives two consecutive probations, they will be dismissed from the program.
Course Drop and Withdrawal:
Course Drop:
A student may drop a course within the specified timeframe without incurring additional fees. The deadline for course drops is mentioned in the semester schedule.
Course Withdrawal:
A student may withdraw from a course before the second sessional exam but will be required to pay the course fee when retaken. The deadline for withdrawals is also listed in the semester schedule.
Code of Conduct and Campus Discipline
Classroom Etiquette:
Punctuality is expected, and students must focus during lectures.
Mobile phones must be switched off; no SMS or messaging is allowed during class.
Any form of misbehavior in class will not be tolerated.
Examination Conduct:
CUI has a strict policy against cheating or the use of unethical means during examinations. Any violation is subject to severe penalties.
Written assignments may be subjected to plagiarism checks using anti-plagiarism software provided by the Higher Education Commission of Pakistan (HEC).
Campus Rules:
CUI Attock is a
NO SMOKING
campus. Students must adhere to this rule at all times.
Discipline must be maintained on campus, and any act of indiscipline may result in severe consequences based on the severity of the misconduct.

Bachelor of Science in Accounting and Finance
Home
Undergraduate
Bachelor of Science in Accounting and Finance
Bachelor of Sciences in Accounting and Finance
Program Overview
“BS Accounting and Finance”
blends together accounting and finance in business organization. This program aims to produce high quality graduates who are both critical and innovative. It would further aim to produce high technical skills as well as well-developed and polished decision making and problem solving skills. The program will be structured around four core areas of Accounting, Finance, Business and Economics.
Accounting:
Financial and management accounting will be studies from a local as well as international perspective. Courses like taxation and auditing will also be offered to give the graduates an insight in to the accounting practices.
Finance:
A thorough understanding of principles of corporate finance, financial institutions and investment will be provided so that the student can adapt themselves to the ever evolving financial markets.
Business and Economics:
A complete understanding of the principles of business will be developed by studying such subjects as marketing, management, communications and information technology.
At the moment the Accountancy and Finance industry is experiencing a severe shortage of experts and trained workforce, which is resulting in shortage of qualified personals in both Accountancy & Finance in Pakistan and the world at large. This program would help to form the basis for collaboration and support by closely working with the certification bodies. The department is trying to take exemptions from ACCA, ICMA and CIMA for the graduating students of this program, by which the students will only have to appear in few modules to get another certification. Another benefit of this program would be the acquisition of a university degree as well as the certification form reputed body.
Special features and objective
A primary objective of this degree is to develop knowledgeable and capable executives to move quickly to key positions in the financial/accounting services sector and to demonstrate the skills necessary to tackle problems within the complex world of international finance and accountancy. Also it is to prepare and implement findings directed at the evaluation of corporate, market, investment and risk management situations. Following are the key objectives.
A systematic understanding of knowledge in accountancy and finance and provision of interface between the knowledge and practice.
A critical awareness of current problems and new insights in Accountancy and finance.
A comprehensive practical understanding of the techniques of enquiry and research used in the sector, and of how they are used to create and interpret knowledge
This program prepares them to proceed onwards to a more targeted certification program in Accounting and Finance along with other program of business administration & management sciences.
Admission and Eligibility
Session:
The program is offered in Fall (September) and Spring (February) Session
Qualification:
Intermediate or equivalent (‘A’ Level) with minimum 50% marks from accredited institution is required for admission in BS(AF) program.
Test and Score:
NTS-NAT test score with minimum 50% marks.
Duration & Semesters:
The minimum duration for the completion of this degree is eight semesters (04 Years) and a maximum of twelve semesters (06 Years). The degree will be awarded on completion of minimum 135 credits with a CGPA of at least 2.0/4.
Documents Required:
Following documents must be attached with the admission form:
Demand Draft in favor of CUI Islamabad from any bank.
MATRIC / O-Level mark sheet certificate & Equivalence, (photocopy back to back).
FA/FSc / A-Level mark sheet, certificate & Equivalence (photocopy back to back).
Copy of NIC / B form.
Valid NTS Result (photocopy) [if test already given].
Paid original copy of NTS Challan Form, [if NTS test not given].
Hope Certificate/Affidavit (To be notarized on Rs. 20/- Stamp Paper) mandatory for result awaiting applicants only.
Undertaking (To be notarized on Rs. 20/- Stamp Paper) mandatory for all applicants.

Bachelor of Science in Mathematics with Data Science
Home
Undergraduate
Bachelor of Science in Mathematics with Data Science
Bachelor of Science in Mathematics with Data Science
The Bachelor of Science in Mathematics with a focus on Data Science is a perfect direction for ambitious students, merging essential and advanced mathematical concepts with foundational data science principles. This program’s curriculum covers crucial areas in mathematics, statistics, data analysis, and computing, enriched with practical applications from real-world business and industry scenarios. Students build a strong grounding in the mathematics underpinning machine learning (ML) and artificial intelligence (AI), equipping them to analyze data, create algorithms, and employ various data science techniques. Graduates are highly prepared for further academic pursuits or careers that require robust quantitative and data analysis expertise, particularly in fields dealing with large-scale data and complex analytics.
The idea in the degree is characterized by important mathematical concepts, combined with applications relevant for providing the techniques and tools to analyze and develop new algorithms and techniques in data science and machine learning. The degree prepares students for further study or for professional and managerial careers, particularly in areas requiring the application of data analysis, dealing with big data and quantitative skills.

Department of Computer Science
Home
About Us CS
About Us
The mission of the Computer Science Department at CUI Attock is to provide degree programs and courses to meet the full range of needs of the talented students in the area of Information Sciences and Technology. Departmental programs are based on a common core curriculum and rationally demanding courses designed by leading experts that supports the breadth of the discipline. Courses in the core curriculum typically have a substantial faculty-directed hands-on component in the form of a regularly scheduled laboratory(s). Departmental degree programs provide the background and experiences appropriate for entering the workplace or a variety of graduate programs at certain levels of intensity. The purpose is ensured by preparing students to work and think independently to generate solutions of the real time problems and projects. Moreover they are encouraged to present new ideas and extend the industrial linkages for enhancement of professional and practical abilities. This practice helps graduates to find jobs in local and international markets. The aim focuses on the professional grooming and skill development of the students who should be able to excel in the field of Computer and Emerging Sciences.

Message from the Head of Department CS
Home
Hods
Message from the Head of Department CS
by
January 11, 2026
Hods
It is a matter of pride and pleasure for me to introduce the Department of Computer Science, COMSATS University Islamabad, Attock campus. Sitting squarely in the Faculty of Information Science and Technology, the department is focused on devising innovative, correct solutions to real life problems, while ensuring a level of excellence in the research and academia, providing world class learning environment. The Department of Computer Science (CS), CUI has been ranked at 1st position in Computer Science and IT category, among all 132 universities of Pakistan by Higher Education Commission (HEC). The BS in Computer Science program is accredited by National Computing Education Accreditation Council (NCEAC).
Our success is evident from our high points such as highly professional, foreign qualified and experienced faculty, diverse degree programs, research achievements and successful alumni serving the top organization nation and world wide. We have eight full-time PhD faculty members supervising in the diverse research domains such as E-Learning, Data mining, Web Mining, Image Processing, Networks, Internet of Things, Artificial Intelligence, Ant Colony Optimization, etc.
The degree programs offered by the department are as follows:
Master of Science in Computer Science
Master of Computer Science
Bachelor of Science (Computer Science)
Bachelor of Science (Software Engineering)
We welcome students who want to make an ace in their life with sheer commitment, dedication and hard work. I hope you will enjoy being a part our proud family and will enjoy our website and look forward for your suggestions and comments.
Sincerely, and with best wishes,
Dr. Zahoor-ur-Rehman Tanoli
Tenured Associate Professor
Head of Department

Department of Computer Science

Vision & Mission CS
Vision & Mission
Vision
To establish a platform that nurtures the growth of computing professionals, provide conducive research environment for faculty, and strengthens partnerships with industry.
Mission
Provide student-centred learning experiences that integrate theoretical foundations with practical applications.
Support and empower faculty in their pursuit of innovative research, creative endeavours, and industry partnerships.
Foster partnerships with the tech industry, government, and community organizations to address real-world challenges and contribute towards socioeconomic growth of the country.

Accreditation CS
Accreditation
National Computing Education Accreditation Council (NCEAC)
NCEAC as an accreditation authority has been setup by Higher Education Commission (HEC) to monitor the quality of computing education. NCEAC periodically visits institutes to assess the standards followed in different Universities, Degree Awarding Institutions and their affiliated colleges offering computing degree programs.
CUI Attock’s BS(CS) 4-years program has been accredited by National Computing Education accreditation council till 2018 while accreditation process For BS(SE) program is in progress
Visit NCEAC at following link,
www.nceac.org

Department of Computer Science
Home
Research Groups CS
Research Groups
Following is the list of Research Groups of our department
Internet, Communications and Networks (ICNet)Research Group
Pattern Recognition Images and Data Engineering (PRIDE)
Software Engineering Research Group (SERG)
Internet, Communications and Networks (ICNet)Research Group
ICNet Research Group was established by the Department of Computer Sciences in 2014. The main objective of ICNet is to promote the atmosphere of research in the area of computer networks. Our research covers a broad range of topics in networking, including network protocols and architecture, modeling and analysis, sensor networks, Vehicular Ad hoc Networks (VANETS), Mobile Ad hoc Networks (MANETS), and Future Internet. At ICNet, there is a scholastic association between teachers and students, aiming to work on ongoing research projects and to explore the potential areas for future work. At ICNet, we welcome high exploratory and speculative proposals in terms of developing the potential for distinctive research in this particular area. We seek a meticulous understanding of current and emerging areas through a harmonious mix of theoretical and applied experimental research.
CONTACT
Dr. Peer Azmat Shah
Dr. Khalid M. Awan
Mr. Mehr Yahya Durrani
Mr. Shehzad Rizwan
Mr. FarhanAadil
Mr. Rehan Tariq
Mr. Usman Anwar
Mr. Umair Khan
Mr.Qasim Jan
Mr.GhassanHasnain
Mr. HashimRazaBukhari
2-PATTERN RECOGNITION IMAGES AND DATA ENGINEERING-PRIDE
PRIDE was established by the Department of Computer Sciences in 2014. Key role of the research group is to develop a conducive research atmosphere in the area of Pattern recognition and Data Engineering. Teachers and students work in collaboration exploring and identifying the potential areas of research in the respective fields. Pattern recognition deals with processing of raw measurement data to arrive at a prediction, which can then be used to determine a decision or action to take. It includes text and image classification, information retrieval and development of recommender systems. Data engineering focuses on methods & techniques for knowledge discovery in databases, data mining and data analysis, and on modern technologies of data warehousing. We try to address these areas through productive research and analysis.
Members:
Dr. Farman Marwat (Group Leader) Dr. Khalid Iqbal
Mr. Armughan Ali
Dr. Salabat khan
Mr. Hikmatullah khan
Ch. Muhammad Shahzad Faisal
Mr. Faisal Shahzad
Mr. Yasir Ali shah
Mr. Shahid Iqbal
Mr. Waqas Ahmed
3-SOFTWARE ENGINEERING RESEARCH GROUP – SERG
Software engineering research group was developed by the Department of Computer Sciences in 2014. SERG actively involves in the research efforts aiming to improve the software modeling techniques, methods and tools to develop complex software systems. Current research areas include software quality assurance, software testing, fault localization, computation and performance analysis and social aspects of software engineering. Students and teachers are working conjointly on current research projects and identifying potential areas for future research. At SERG teachers not only collaborate with students in their post graduate research but also discuss their own ongoing research in their respective areas of interests.
Members:
Dr. Saqib Iqbal (Group Leader)
Mr. Fawad
Mr. Usman
Mr. Shahzad Rizwan

Salabat Khan, Waseem Shahzad, Farrukh Aslam, “Cryptanalysis of Four-Rounded Data Encryption Standard using Binary Ant Colony Optimization”, International Conference on Information Science and Applications (ICISA), IEEE, pp. 1-7, 2010.
Muhammad Sharif, Mohsin Bilal, Salabat Khan, M. Arfan Jaffar, “Adaptive Structuring Element and Morphological Operators using Binary PSO”, Lecture Notes in Computer Science, vol. 6377/2010, pp. 525-532, 2010.
Salabat Khan, Mohsin Bilal, M. Sharif, Farrukh Aslam, Ahsan Abdullah, “Crossing Minimization of Bipartite Graph Using Genetic Algorithm – BDP”, (Accepted in ICSI 2010, China)
Zahid Halim, A. Rauf Baig and Salabat Khan, “Modular Indoor Games: A Hybrid of Video and Outdoor Games”, International Conference on Computational Intelligence and Software Engineering (CiSE), Wuhan, China, December 11-13, 2009.
Salabat Khan, Mohsin Bilal, M. Sharif, Malik Sajid, Rauf Baig, “Solution of n-Queen Problem Using ACO”, International Multitopic Conference, Islamabad, IEEE, pp. 1-5, 2009.
Majid Qayyum M., S Jabbar., F Azam and S Rizwan. 2012. “Stagnant Free Ant Based Energy Aware Heuristic Routing In Wireless Sensor Network”. In preceedings of IEEE International conference (CMSSN-12), Denver, Colorado USA.
“Analyzing the effects of Mobility Models Pattern in Mobile Ad hoc Network” has been accepted for inclusion in the preceedings of International Conference on Information and Communication Technologies (ICICT-2008) at University of Science & Technology Bannu Pakistan.
“A Simulation based performance comparison of Group and Entity Mobility Models in Mobile Ad hoc Networks” has accepted for preceedings of 8th National Research Conference (NRC-2009) at SZABIST University Islamabad Pakistan.
ZahoorurRehman, M.Shahbaz, M. Shaheen, Aziz Guergachi., “Situation-awareness and Sensor Stream Mining for Sustainable Society” (2009) International Conference on Soft Computing and Pattern Recognition (Malaysia) ISBN-13: 978-0-7695-3879-2
ZahoorurRehman, M. Imran, M.Aslam, M. Shaheen., “An Intelligent Mathematical Production Assistant” (2009) ACM International Conference on Frontier of Information Technology

Muhammad Shaheen, Zahoor Ur Rehman “Critical Skills for Computer Academicians” (2008) Proceedings of Informing Science Society Vol:- pp:405-421 (Conference Publications)

, Nasir Ahmad, Muhammad Naeem, Proceedings of the 18th International Conference on Automation & Computing, Loughborough University, Leicestershire, UK, 8 September 2012, Pages 119-122.

Resources CS
Library
The Library at CUI, Attock campus is spacious, well planned, and offers tranquil environment. It is fast developing into one of the richest information resource center in Attock. The library subscribes to a good number of periodicals and journals, which have educational value for students. In addition, it also offers its users a rich learning environment complemented with electronic information access and services. The library has circulation, reserve and reference sections. Internet facilities in the library connect users to libraries around the world for reference, assistance and consultation. The library is fully equipped with sophisticated audiovisual system. Students are encouraged to make use of the educational material available on videotapes, CDs, DVDs as well as on audiotapes. Students can search for resources using state of the art computerized library catalogue system. A portion of the library has been designated as silence-area, providing students with ideal environment for studies. The stock and services of the Library though directed mainly towards professionals teaching staff and students, is however, open to all departments & faculties’ employees.
Library Resources:
The CUI Attock Library has the following resources
Books:
Engineering Books : 3100
Management Science : 1600
Computer Science : 1400
Mathematics : 600
General Books : 400
Books from HEC (e-library): 40,000
Virtual University CDs: 1100
Virtual University Video Cassettes: 500
CDs with Books: 1100
Digital Library:
The CUI Attock Library is a regular user of the HEC Digital Library. The Library user can access more than 30,000 online Journals / Magazines. HEC Digital Library offers the following links to access the digital resources:
Institute of Electrical and Electronic Engineers (IEEE)
Association of Computing Machinery (ACM)
Cambridge University Press (CUP )
Emerald
JSTOR
Science Direct
ISI Web of Knowledge
Palgrave Macmillan
American Association of Physics Teachers
American Institute of Physics
American Mathematical Society
American Physical Society
American Society of Microbiology
Institute of Physics
The Institute of Engineering and Technology (IET)
Nature Publication
Computer Labs
There are – labs throughout the campus, out of which 6 are dedicated to the department of CS. Our labs are equipped with Computers with Intel i3 and i7 processors 3.40 GHz, 4 to 8 GB RAM, 512 GB hard disk, interconnected with high speed Ethernet network. Computing facilities is equally available to faculty, research associates, and students.
CL-1,2
Location:
Academic Block 1 – 1st Floor
Hardware Specification:
Processor: Intel(R) Core(TM) i7-6700 CPU 3.41 GHz.
Installed memory (RAM): 8.00 GB.
Hard Drive: 512 GB.
Software Installed:
Windows 10 Enterprise, Microsoft Office 2013, MS Visio 2013, Smadav Antivirus Virus, Bloodshed Dev-C++, Matlab R2018b, NASM, NetBeans 8.1, MySQL Workbench, Packet Tracer, SQL Server 2014, VmWare 9.0, Ubuntu 14, WinRar, Ecllipse, Foxit Reader, Python, Star UML, Sublime, Wampp Server.

Message from the Head of Department EE
Home
Hods
Message from the Head of Department EE
by
January 9, 2026
Hods
Since inception, the department has been producing world class graduates and postgraduates. The state of the art infrastructure and lab facilities are established with grants from different agencies which ensure good exposure and hands on experience for students during learning process. The students have been employed in top core and engineering companies. Every year a good number of students go to higher studies in well-reputed universities abroad. The faculty of the department has been involved in several research projects in cutting edge technologies and publications in many international journals and conferences.
The global climate change and depleting natural resources are demanding invention of new technologies which are energy conscious. The confidence in managing new knowledge society requires continuous learning through novel approaches supported with research and development in the areas of power and energy. Thus, the department vision and mission reflect this, and my department joins me in meeting this mission by producing knowledgeable and committed technologists to serve our country and humanity as a whole. The hard work and sincerity are strong pillars of success. Through our practices we strive to impress our students to inculcate these values and support the mission of COMSATS University Islamabad. I welcome wholeheartedly our alumni to join hands in supporting our endeavors by all means of interaction. Our doors are always open to universities, research organizations, industries and utility companies to collaborate with us in building valuable knowledge society foreseeing bright future.
Dr. Yasir Muhammad
Assistant Professor
Head, Department of Electrical and Computer Engineering,
COMSATS University Islamabad, Attock Campus

About Us EE
Home
About Us EE
About Us
The Department of Electrical Engineering (EE) in Attock campus was established in 2007. The EE department aims to achieve academic and research excellence in the subject area through its well-designed curriculum, strong focus on research and innovation, objective based learning and strong industrial liaison. Moreover, the department believes and strives to provide excellent facilities, best teaching methods and a learning environment for the students to achieve professional and academic excellence.
Since its inception in 2007, the department of electrical and computer engineering has successfully launched multiple degree programs, including Ph.D. electrical engineering, Ph.D. computer engineering, MS electrical engineering, BS electrical engineering, and BS computer engineering in a short span of time. The curriculum of these programs encompasses the vast background of electrical and computer engineering. The ECE department offers a wide range of elementary as well as advanced courses pertaining to the broad range of specialized courses including electrical power, telecommunications, electronics, computer and embedded systems. To provide students with the research and internship opportunities, CUI has strong collaboration with Pakistan Aeronautical Complex (PAC) Kamra under a Memorandum of Understanding.

Vision and Mission EE
Vision and Mission
Vision of the University:
The COMSATS University Islamabad envisions assuming a truly national character for itself in the years to come. It envisions having presence in all provinces of the country. It sees for itself a position among the top five (5) universities in the country; among top 100 universities in the developing countries and top 300, 200, 100 universities in the world respectively in the 5, 10 and 15 years’ time horizon.
Mission of the University:
The COMSATS University Islamabad founded in the belief that understanding enriches all people, is dedicated to the search for truth through advancement of learning and extending the frontiers of knowledge; to the sharing of this knowledge through education in an academically diverse range of disciplines and subjects; and to the application of this knowledge to benefit the people of Pakistan, in particular, and the
Muslim Ummah, and the world, at large. The University’s mission is threefold:
• Research and Discovery:
Generate and preserve knowledge, understanding, and creativity by triggering enquiry, conducting high- quality research, and promoting scholarship, that benefit students, scholars, and communities across the country, the Muslim Ummah, and the World, at large.
• Teaching and Learning:
Share that knowledge, understanding, and creativity by providing a broad range of educational programs in a diverse community of learners and teachers, and prepare graduate, professional, and undergraduate students, as well as non-degree seeking students interested in continuing education and lifelong learning, and for assuming active roles in competitive and culturally diverse environs.
• Outreach and Public Service:
Extend, apply, and exchange knowledge between the University and society by applying scholarly expertise to social and technological problems, by helping organizations and individuals respond to their changing environments and by making the knowledge and resources created and preserved at the University accessible to the citizens. Using the resources of its multiple campuses in an integrated fashion, the University vies to strengthen the services to the state through the education of a modern work force, research and development, technology commercialization, and establishing and promoting partnerships with business, government and community groups.
Vision
“To be recognized globally as one of the leading departments of electrical engineering education.”
Mission
“To prepare competent electrical engineering graduates conscious of professional ethical and social responsibilities for productive engineering careers in industry, academia, and research both locally and abroad.”

Code of Conduct EE
Code of Conduct
As students of the premier institution of higher learning, students are expected to adhere to a Code of Conduct and maintain a certain degree of decorum and etiquette while they are on campus. Students are strongly encouraged, as partners/stakeholders of the CUI community, to take an active part in observing the code of conduct spelt out in the succeeding lines, so as to uphold the dignity and good name of the Institution
Students’ Attire
Students not displaying the ID cards will be fined Rs. 200/- and the card will be confiscated until the challan form is submitted.
To maintain the good image of the institution, students are required to be properly and decently attired when they are on campus. A smart and presentable bearing is in order.
Improper attire includes indecently revealing shorts, shabbily fitted jeans, pants with too many pockets (cargo pants), Bedroom attire, clothes carrying indecent words or pictures on them that are offensive to others, Slippers. The male students are also not allowed to wear jewelry such as Chains, Bracelets, Anklets, friendship bands etc. All the students should be decently dressed.
Students who are sloppily dressed up will not be allowed to attend classes, labs and libraries. In faculty and administrative offices, students who are not properly attired will not be served and their names will be taken down and sent to the respective Chairman and the Office of Student Affairs for records.
Smoking
The CUI Attock is a ‘No-Smoking’ campus. The penalty for breaching this rule for the first time is a fine of Rs.1000/-, second time the fine of Rs.5, 000/- and suspension for the whole semester. Use of Hand Phones /Pagers/Digital Diaries/music players. Use of Mobile Phones/Camera Phones or playing music on mobile phones, mp3 players or any other device is prohibited in the Academic Area, Classrooms, and Corridors. In case of violations, the Phone will be confiscated, or a fine may be imposed
Disorderly/Offensive Behavior
As members of the CUI Community, students are encouraged to set an exemplary standard regarding their conduct. Their impeccable conduct always would be in consonance with their status as part of this community. As such, CUI will take disciplinary action against any student who is guilty of physical abuse, participation in a disturbance of the peace or pose a threat to the safety and security of any member(s) of CUI community. A penalty in the shape of a fine or suspension, whatever is deemed necessary by the concerned Proctor, will be given on noticing disorderly/offensive behavior.
VANDALISM, MUTILATION AND THEFT OF BOOKS
All acts of vandalism, mutilation and theft of CUI property/ individual’s property will be dealt with severe punishments. A student found guilty is liable to be suspended from the CUI or as deemed necessary by the Proctor.
Littering
Students are urged to play an active part in keeping our campus and public places clean. It is in our interest to have a clean environment. As part of gracious living, students are encouraged to use public property in the same manner as they treat their own. Your cooperation and understanding is sought in disposing the different waste materials in the appropriate manner or waste bins. Our social habits reflect our progress towards a gracious society.
Gambling
The playing of any game of chance or mixed game of chance and skill shall be strictly prohibited in the precincts of CUI. Any student who contravenes this rule shall be subject to disciplinary proceedings and upon being found guilty of contravening this rule, shall be liable to punishment as deemed by the Proctor or in an intense case by the Chief Proctor.
Conduct Unbecoming
Students are advised to desist from bullying around to peck order, casting aspersions or slurs on other students and initiating any form of conduct through speech or body language that causes embarrassment, humiliation or loss of dignity or well-being to another student.
General
The Proctors assigned for ensuring the proper observation of the above-mentioned Code will also look after the following decree:
Failure to properly identify oneself
Lying to a Proctor during an official investigation
Dress/hair code violation: male or female
Failure to respond to an official call slip within 48 hours
Horseplay
Vandalism or Damaging CUI property
Improper personal contact
Direct disobedience/disrespect with faculty, staff and Proctors
Entering entryway of opposite sex on campus or allowing the same
Gambling
Improper social behavior
Obscene, profane or abusive language or behavior
Participation in an unauthorized demonstration
Possession and/or viewing of pornography
Possession of an Institution/Room/Lab etc. key without authorization
Safety/security violation
Falsification of information on an official document
Racial, ethnic, sectarian, gender harassment
Violation of silence zones i.e., near faculty offices, lecture halls, design studios, labs, and libraries.
Shouting/talking noisily in corridors and stairs in such a way that it disturbs the overall academic environment.
Sitting on the stairs or in the corridors in such a way that it blocks the way for passers-by.
Any misbehavior with other students, faculty, staff or guards.
Threat to do bodily harm
Possession or consumption of alcoholic beverages
Stealing or possession of stolen property
Possession/use of weapons
Important:
The CUI will not interfere with any action that the police may deem necessary to take against some serious lapses on the part of students.

Accreditation EE
Accreditation
Pakistan Engineering Council (PEC)
Pakistan Engineering Council (PEC) team visited CUI Attock campus on April 16, 2012 for zero visit of Computer Engineering program. Green signal was granted to launch the program in 63rd EA and QEC meeting held on June 23, 2012.
PEC team visited CUI Attock campus on August 11, 2015 for interim visit of Computer Engineering program. The campus is waiting for accreditation status from PEC.
PEC team visited CUI Attock campus on April 28, 2011 for zero visit of Electrical Engineering program. Green signal was granted to launch the program in 61st EA and QEC meeting.
PEC team visited CUI Attock campus on April 16, 2012 for Interim visit of Electrical Engineering program. Green signal was granted to continue the program in 63rd EA and QEC meeting.
PEC team visited CUI Attock campus on June 04, 2013 for change of scope (increase in intake).
PEC team visited CUI Attock campus on March 19, 2014 for change of scope (increase in intake).
PEC team visited CUI Attock campus on Feb 19, 2015 for Accreditation of Electrical Engineering program.
PEC accredited Electrical Engineering department.

Research Groups EE
Research Groups
Following is the list of Research Groups of our department
OPTRIC (Optimization Research and Innovation Center)
OPTRIC researchers carry out advanced studies in the solution of difficult, large-scale optimization problems, with special focus on state-of-the-art implementation of modern algorithms. We are primarily interested in the solution of problems with practical relevance, and we actively seek collaboration with industrial partners.
ACRC (Antenna & Communication Research Center)
ACRC bring together the research excellence of individuals and groups across the university. The Antenna & Communication Research Centre specializes in the analysis, design and measurement of antennas and associated devices for wireless communications. With several years of applied research experience and it has the capability to build an international reputation for innovative futuristic concepts and solutions to contemporary industrial challenges.

Research Publications EE

Resources EE
Academic Resources
Library
The Library at CUI, Attock campus is spacious, well planned, and offers tranquil environment. It is fast developing into one of the richest information resource center in Attock. The library subscribes to a good number of periodicals and journals, which have educational value for students. In addition, it also offers its users a rich learning environment complemented with electronic information access and services. The library has circulation, reserve and reference sections. Internet facilities in the library connect users to libraries around the world for reference, assistance and consultation. The library is fully equipped with sophisticated audiovisual system. Students are encouraged to make use of the educational material available on videotapes, CDs, DVDs as well as on audiotapes. Students can search for resources using state of the art computerized library catalogue system. A portion of the library has been designated as silence-area, providing students with ideal environment for studies. The stock and services of the Library though directed mainly towards professionals teaching staff and students, is however, open to all departments & faculties’ employees.
Library Resources:
The CUI Attock Library has the following resources
Books

Digital Library:
The CUI Attock Library is a regular user of the HEC Digital Library. The Library user can access more than 30,000 online Journals / Magazines. HEC Digital Library offers the following links to access the digital resources:

Computer Labs
There are – labs throughout the campus, out of which 9 are dedicated to the department of CS. Our labs are equipped with Computers with Intel i3 processor 2.4 to 2.6 GHz, 2 to 4 GB RAM, 256 to 512 GB hard disk, interconnected with high speed Ethernet network. Computing facilities is equally available to faculty, research associates, and students.
CONTROLS LAB
Mission Statement /Vision
Control and Simulation Lab is of significant interest in most areas of industry especially in Electrical and Computer Engineering world- new and established setups. The applications in Control Systems world plays an increasingly important role in the developing world, making it crucial for the students to be exposed to contemporary control system equipment in a realistic manner. The lab is equipped with advanced soft wares like Lab VIEW and MATLAB. These software are ‘higher-level’ technical computing languages that provide a platform for algorithm development, data analysis, data visualization of Control theories and principles. Main Topics which are covered given below
Controller design
Controller tests on the model
Controller implementation in real-time applications
Implementation of various control strategies
Functional Profile:
The functional profile of the lab is given below:
Overview of Controls and Simulation Lab:
DC-Motor:
The Quanser Engineering Trainers for NI ELVIS (QNET) DC Motor Control Trainer is designed to illustrate the fundamentals of DC motor control by configuring motor position and speed, parameter estimation, and control of a haptic knob. Using QNET hardware-in-the-loop implementations, engineering students can complement their laboratory work with hands-on, practical experience in the important aspects of engineering practice, which spurs student interest and motivation.
Rotary Pendulum:
The Quanser Engineering Trainers for NI ELVIS (QNET) Rotary Inverted Pendulum Trainer gives students the ability to experiment with classic pendulum control challenges. By designing a control system that balances a vertical rod at the tip of a rotating arm, students gain intuition on control topics such as system modeling, parameter estimation, balance control, linear-quadratic regulator (LQR) design, nonlinear swing-up control, and energy-based design. The plant features a DC servo motor, built-in power amplifier, and optical encoders to sense the position of the pendulum.
Control system Lab Research:
Taking advantage of the NI ELVIS pedagogical platform, DC Motor has developed six (6) specialized plants with the necessary experiments to teach controls topics throughout an engineering course. Each of these add-on boards plug directly into the NI ELVIS and transform NI ELVIS from teaching circuits and taking measurements, into an effective controls platform.Using QNET hardware-in-the-loop implementations, engineering students can complement their laboratory work with hands-on, practical experience in the important aspects of engineering practice, which spurs student interest and motivation. QNETs for NI ELVIS provide the components educators need to set up their control design, simulation, mechatronics/optics, dynamics, or thermodynamics lab.
Accreditation:
PEC
People:
Mr. Saad Zahid, Mr. Shamroz Aslam & Mr. Mubashir Rehman
COMMUNICATION LAB
Mission Statement /Vision
The NI USRP platform offers new opportunities for RF and communications education, which traditionally has been focused on mathematical theory. Students can use the platform with LabVIEW to link theory and practical implementation through hands-on execution and exploration of a working communications system using live signals.
Functional Profile
Overview
The NI USRP-2922 software defined radio (SDR) transceiver is an affordable and easy-to-use RF platform for rapidly prototyping applications in wireless communications research and education. It has continuous frequency coverage from 400 MHz to 4.4 GHz that includes some of the most commonly researched technologies such as cellular, GNSS, 2.4 GHz WiFi, L band radar, and S band radar. This SDR device allows simultaneous transmit and receive with up to 40 MHz of instantaneous bandwidth. The integrated multiple input, multiple output (MIMO) and synchronization port enables plug-and-play 2×2 MIMO. The external reference clock inputs allow the synchronization of up to eight devices for 8×8 MIMO or higher-channel-count direction-finding applications.
Communications Research:
Lab VIEW provides a scalable platform for communications research that bridges design and test. Designers can seamlessly share code between the rapid prototyping NI USRP (Universal Software Radio Peripheral) platform and the test hardware PXI RF platform. The NI-proven reference designs provide an excellent start to any research application, and the LabVIEW multiple models of computation make it possible to leverage existing code written in a .m file script or in C.
Example Applications:
Low-cost RF modulated source–synthesize I/Q waveforms
Reproduction of a previously recorded RF signal
Physical layer prototyping–algorithm development
Channel modeling and characterization
GPS record and playback
WiFi beacon and packet decoding
Spectrum monitoring
MIMO communications and direction finding
NI USRP-2922 Kit Contents:
NI USRP-2922 device with international power supply
Modulation Toolkit
LabVIEW Digital Filter Design Toolkit
LabVIEW Math Script RT Module
3 m Ethernet cable
0.3 m SMA-SMA loopback cable
30 dB SMA inline attenuator
Professional Accreditation:
PEC
People:
Mr. Bilal Khan, Mr. Abbas Ali Shah, Mr. Wasiq Ali
DIGITAL LOGIC DESIGN / MICROPROCESSOR LAB
Mission Statement /Vision
This lab is designed to provide an atmosphere for both electrical and computer engineering students and the fundamental concepts like digital logic methods of analysis, design of digital logic devices and microprocessor systems. Students are able to achieve and develop an understanding of digital logic based circuits and systems. Furthermore, this lab provides analysis and synthesizes of logic networks using both traditional techniques (such as K-maps and State Tables) and use of modern LabVeiw tools. Students can get hands on experience after using the latest and modern instruments which is installed in this lab.
Functional Profile
Overview:
Students of Electrical and Computer Engineering programs are involved in projects that are related with DLD/MP in engineering design and application. These students perform substantive lab work to gain practical and hands-on engineering experience on the installed latest equipment(s) and the software(s). In order to meet project demands, the DLD/MP lab is equipped with latest equipment such as E-Pal -27 (advance digital Electronic Trainers), MTS-86C (Microcontroller Trainer Board), FPGA Kits (Spartan 6 & Vertix 6), Easy Pic6 Micro Controller Kits (Micro Electronika), Universal Programmer. Also to integrate these devices with different latest software’s, Students in the DLD/MP Lab are provided with PCs along with printing as well as internet facility.
Key Features:
Plug-and-play design enables quick & easy lab setup
Facilitates a diverse range of DLD/MP experiments that illustrate an array of curriculum concepts
Compact & easy to implement
Pre-packaged with comprehensive curriculum materials that reduce lab planning requirements
Fully compatible with E-Pal & LAB VIEW 2012
Unparalleled academic-based technical support
Projects:
Mobile Phone Detector
Lie Detector
Digital Clock with on-off timer
Fire Sensing System
Digital Lock
Automatic Gate Light
Rain Sound Generator
Water level indicator
Traffic Light Signal
Courses:
Digital Logic Design (2nd Semester)
Microprocessor systems and Interface (5th Semester)
Advance Digital Logic Design (6th Semester)
Computer Organization Architecture (5th Semester)
Advance Digital System Design (MS)
VLSI (7th Semester)
Real Time Embedded Systems (7th Semester)
ELECTRONICS / ECA LAB
Mission Statement /Vision
The mission of the Electronics/ECA laboratory is to provide an environment to the students at EE department where they can perform the most basic as well as the advanced experiments related to electronic circuits. In addition to this, students are introduced to the functionality and usage of state of the art electronic test equipment.
Functional Profile
This lab supports the practical experiments of the multiple courses including Electronics I, Electronics II, Electric Circuit Analysis (ECA) I and II. There are 20 workstations equipped with the technologically advanced equipment including Oscilloscopes, Arbitrary Waveform Generators, Semi-conductor Curve Tracer and D-A Training System. These workstations are the best known for their ability to verify the concepts of digital and analog electronics.Additionally, each workstation is also equipped with a PC containing the advanced software including PSPICE and Electronic Workbench to simulate and validate the electronic circuits.
Professional Accreditation/ Affiliations
Physics lab fulfills all the requirements conforming to the standards set by Pakistan Engineering Council (PEC) as well as Quality Enhancement Cell (QEC).
People:
Lab In-charge: Mr. Hassan Saeed Qazi
ELECTRICAL MEASUREMENTS & INSTRUMENTATION LAB
Mission Statement /Vision
Measurement is the process or the result of determining the magnitude of a quantity, such as length or mass, relative to a unit of measurement, such as a meter or a kilogram. EMI lab comprises of measuring instruments and devices for performing various experiments related to measurement of important electrical parameters like voltage, current, power, energy, frequency, inductance and capacitance etc.
Functional Profile
Overview
To provide students with basic Measurement techniques using electronic Instruments and support Electrical and Computer Engineering general hands-on teaching and sensitive current measurement. Build intuition by taking models from simulation to implementation using one software platform. Save time with comprehensive curriculum that enables a deep understanding of engineering principles.
Key Features:
Plug-and-play design enables quick & easy lab setup
Facilitates a diverse range of controls experiments that illustrate an array of curriculum concepts
Compact & easy to store
Pre-packaged with comprehensive curriculum materials that reduce lab planning requirements
Fully compatible with NI ELVIS & Lab VIEW
Unparalleled academic-based technical support
EM&I Research:
Quanser’s modular range of control hardware allows you to use the same peripherals to control a wide variety of mechatronic experiments. The experiments are open-architecture and compatible with LabVIEW™ and MATLAB®/Simulink® to ensure we can conveniently support your unique requirements. Industry-relevant curriculum is included with many cutting-edge work stations that are strategically designed to help teach introductory, intermediate and advanced controls to students in Electrical, Mechanical, Mechatronics, Robotics, Aerospace, Civil and various other engineering disciplines. Several examples of workstations are presented here. Please note that the recommended Data Acquisition Boards shown in this diagram can be replaced by other boards to achieve the desired performance level
PHYSICS LAB
Mission Statement /Vision
Physics lab was established at the very beginning with the help of NVIS Technologies Pvt. Limited with a vision enhancement of the basic concepts of engineering physics and introduction to advanced physical concepts used in Electrical Engineering. This lab provides freshmen with an opportunity to gain practical experience of measurement sciences which is the fundamental part of the engineering programs being taught at the department.
Functional Profile
Physics lab supports the multiple courses including Applied Physics for Engineers by providing implementation and verification of theoretical concepts and laws of Physics. Besides basic components, the major equipment in this lab includes Melde’s apparatus, Gauss and Tesla Meter, LCR Meter, Spectrometer and Halls Effect Trainer in an ample quantity. This lab has 20 work stations which can be used simultaneously and independently.
Professional Accreditation/ Affiliations:
Physics lab fulfills all the requirements conforming to the standards set by Pakistan Engineering Council (PEC) as well as Quality Enhancement Cell (QEC)
People:
Lab In-charge: Mr. Syed Abbas Ali Shah
POWER ELECTRONICS LAB
Mission Statement /Vision
The integration of fast and controlled switching makes Power conversion much easier then past which makes the electronics systems more and more efficient and are responsible for high productivity. These different switching techniques integrated with machines to implement variable speed drives efficiently. These switches are also heart of renewable technologies and green energy.
Functional Profile
Overview
Overview Power Electronics Laboratory is equipped with a Power Electronics Training System by LABVOLT , which includes power MOSFETS, power thyristors, chopper/inverters control units, thyristors controllers, PID controllers, function generators, vector control drive converters, The lab also features data acquisition system, electric machines, such as DC motors, synchronous motors and induction motors. With Computer based metering and control Block.
Key Features:
Plug-and-play design enables quick & easy lab setup
Whole package of power quality analyzer in LV-DAC(EMS) software
Compact & easy to store
Computer based instrumentation and control
Pre-packaged with comprehensive curriculum materials that reduce lab planning requirements
Unparalleled academic-based technical support
Power Electronics Research:
This lab is used for teaching and research topic of the integration of power electronics 3 phase and single phase converters and electric machines to design and implement motor drive systems and control of electromechanical systems automatic power factor correction systems, HVDC systems, Automatic governor controller for three phase synchronous generator.AC and DC motor drives and different topologies involved in drives.
Professional Accreditation:
PEC
People:
Lab Instructors: Rizwan Ullah, Mr. Ejaz Ahmed and Mr Hassan Syed Qazi
ELECTRICAL MACHINES LAB
Mission Statement /Vision
Electrical Machines and Drives play a powerful role in industry with an ever increasing importance. This fact requires the understanding of machine and drive principles by engineers different form of electrical conversions and formulas which are modeling these phenomena there limitations and efficiency.
Functional Profile
Overview:
Our Electrical Machines Laboratory is equipped with a 0.2 kW electromechanical training system by LABVOLT Which includes Four quadrant Dynometer/Power supply, AC and DC machines (DC motors /Generators, 3 Phase synchronous motors/Generators ,Universal Motors ,single phase Split phase and 3 phase induction motors),Single and three phase distribution transformer Three phase Electrical and Mechanical loads , Data Acquisition system, Computer based metering and control Block.
Key Features:
Plug-and-play design enables quick & easy lab setup
Whole package of power quality analyzer in LV-DAC(EMS) software
Compact & easy to store
Computer based instrumentation and control
Pre-packaged with comprehensive curriculum materials that reduce lab planning requirements
Unparalleled academic-based technical support
Electrical Machine Research
This lab is used for teaching and research topic of the integration of power electronics 3 phase and single phase converters and electric machines to design and implement motor drive systems and control of electromechanical systems automatic power factor correction systems, HVDC systems, Automatic governor controller for three phase synchronous generator.AC and DC motor drives and different topologies involved in drives.
Professional Accreditation:
PEC
People:
Lab Instructors: Mr. Rizwan Ullah, Mr. Ejaz Ahmed and Mr Hassan Syed Qazi

About Us CE
About Us
With a vision to produce professional engineering graduates, the Department of Electrical Engineering was established in 2007. The EE department aims to achieve the academic and research excellence in the subject area through its well-designed curriculum, strong focus on research and innovation, objective based learning and strong industrial liaison. Moreover the department believes and strives to provide the excellent facilities, best teaching methods and learning environment to the students in order to achieve professional and academic excellence.
Since its inception in 2007, the Department of Electrical Engineering has successfully launched multiple degree programs, including BS (Electrical Engineering), MS (Electrical Engineering) and BS (Computer Engineering) in a short span of time. The curriculum of these programs encompasses the vast background of electrical and computer engineering. The EE department offers a wide range of elementary as well as advanced courses pertaining to the broad range of specializations including Electrical Power, Telecommunications, Electronics, Computer and Control Systems. In order to provide students with the research and internship opportunities, CUI has strong collaboration with Pakistan Aeronautical Complex (PAC) Kamra under a Memorandum of Understanding.
All engineering programs offered by the department are recognized by Pakistan Engineering Council (PEC) because of the excellent educational standards of CUI and commitment of the faculty.
The major objectives of department are summarized as:
To develop graduates with strong academic foundation in multiple areas of specialization.
To enhance the analytical and problem solving skills of graduates and induce critical thinking.
To inculcate a strong sense of ethics and professionalism in its graduates to make significant and positive contribution to the industry and society at large.

Message from the Head of Department CE

Hods
Message from the Head of Department CE
by
January 10, 2026
Hods
Welcome to the Department of Computer Engineering, where innovation meets excellence in education and research. Since its inception, our department has been committed to producing highly skilled graduates and postgraduates who contribute to cutting-edge technological advancements.
Our department offers a comprehensive range of programs, including BS Computer Engineering, MS Computer Engineering, and PhD Computer Engineering, designed to equip students with the knowledge and skills required to excel in the rapidly evolving field of computing and engineering.
We take pride in our state-of-the-art infrastructure and well-equipped laboratories, established with grants from various agencies, providing students with hands-on experience and exposure to emerging technologies. Our graduates have secured positions in leading engineering and technology firms, while many pursue higher studies at prestigious international universities.
Our faculty is actively engaged in innovative research projects, contributing to high-impact publications and technological advancements in fields such as artificial intelligence, embedded systems and wireless communication.
We believe in fostering an environment that encourages critical thinking, problem-solving, and interdisciplinary collaboration. With our dedicated faculty, modern facilities, and industry-academia linkages, we strive to shape the future of Computer Engineering and empower our students to become leaders, innovators, and change-makers in the digital world.
I invite you to explore the opportunities our department offers and join us in our journey of excellence in teaching, research, and technological innovation.
Best Regards,
Shujaat Ali Khan Tanoli
Head of Department
Department of Computer Engineering
COMSATS University Islamabad – Attock Campus

Vision and Mission CE
Vision and Mission
Department Vision
To be recognized globally as one of the leading departments of engineering education.
Department Mission
To prepare competent electrical and computer engineering graduates conscious of professional ethical and social responsibilities for productive engineering careers in industry, academia, and research both locally and abroad.

Accreditation CE
Accreditation
Pakistan Engineering Council (PEC)
Pakistan Engineering Council (PEC) team visited CUI Attock campus on April 16, 2012 for zero visit of Computer Engineering program. Green signal was granted to launch the program in 63rd EA and QEC meeting held on June 23, 2012.
PEC team visited CUI Attock campus on August 11, 2015 for interim visit of Computer Engineering program. The campus is waiting for accreditation status from PEC.
PEC team visited CUI Attock campus on April 28, 2011 for zero visit of Electrical Engineering program. Green signal was granted to launch the program in 61st EA and QEC meeting.
PEC team visited CUI Attock campus on April 16, 2012 for Interim visit of Electrical Engineering program. Green signal was granted to continue the program in 63rd EA and QEC meeting.
PEC team visited CUI Attock campus on June 04, 2013 for change of scope (increase in intake).
PEC team visited CUI Attock campus on March 19, 2014 for change of scope (increase in intake).
PEC team visited CUI Attock campus on Feb 19, 2015 for Accreditation of Electrical Engineering program.
PEC accredited Electrical Engineering department.

Research Groups CE
Research Groups
Following is the list of Research Groups of our department
OPTRIC (Optimization Research and Innovation Center)
OPTRIC researchers carry out advanced studies in the solution of difficult, large-scale optimization problems, with special focus on state-of-the-art implementation of modern algorithms. We are primarily interested in the solution of problems with practical relevance, and we actively seek collaboration with industrial partners.
ACRC (Antenna & Communication Research Center)
ACRC bring together the research excellence of individuals and groups across the university. The Antenna & Communication Research Centre specializes in the analysis, design and measurement of antennas and associated devices for wireless communications. With several years of applied research experience and it has the capability to build an international reputation for innovative futuristic concepts and solutions to contemporary industrial challenges.
